Your Majesty, having received the Mandate and inaugurated the era, holds the celestial tally and governs the realm. You cultivate civilizing influence to pacify distant lands and display martial prowess to quell the Nine Provinces. Your benevolence encompasses all vegetation, and Your kindness extends even to ants and insects. Remote barbarians untie their braids to embrace benevolence; fierce tribes scale mountains to present tribute. Thus, all beings, even the most alien, are moved by Your grace—snow hares and frost birds nest in close proximity, auspicious dragons and divine turtles appear as commonplace.

Now, at Jade Grotto’s cloud-capped peaks, the sacred site of ancient transformations—where, during the prosperous reign of the Han, the Heavenly Master cultivated the Dao—verdant forests stretch and misty vapors glow. Green cliffs bear the woven patterns of moss, where the celestial chariot’s tracks still linger in the air; emerald glades are carpeted with lush grass, where the alchemical altar of the crane-transformation remains. Yet before these crags stood ancient cypresses, withered and decayed for years. Now, bathed in rain and dew, they have revived in splendor, sprouting golden shoots and flourishing anew. Their towering boughs sway with verdant grace, their dense foliage casting deep shade. Even Wang Yi’s famed camphor trees cannot rival their luxuriance, nor can the immortal cypress of Lai Xiang match their auspiciousness. The revival of these seven cypresses heralds a reign of boundless longevity, a wonder unparalleled in ancient records.

Your servant, privileged to serve in this flourishing era, has frequently witnessed such felicitous omens. Daring to compose verses in celebration, I wish to proclaim Your virtue across the realm. With utmost reverence, I present a seven-character quatrain in four rhymes to extol Your sagely power and offer congratulations.

**Memorial Congratulating the Audience of Western Hu Monks**

Your servant humbly notes that monks from the Western Regions and India have arrived at court to pay homage. Your boundless compassion reaches distant lands, inspiring foreign realms to seek allegiance. Thus, monks from ten thousand *li* away come to pay tribute to a millennium’s sagely sovereign. Chinese and barbarians alike submit to Your transformative influence; all beings rejoice in unison.

Your servant offers his congratulations. Your Majesty, inheriting the sacred lineage and embodying the primordial, establishes the ultimate standard. Your benevolence blankets the Nine Lands, bestowing blessings upon all; Your governance extends to the Eight Wildernesses, fostering harmony and prosperity. Thus, all regions present tribute, and interpreters throng the court. Tribute arrives without fail each month, and chroniclers’ records never cease.

Now, from the distant Western Hu, beyond the snowy deserts and shifting sands, near the towering peaks and isles of deer, they gaze upon the clouds reaching the heavens and conceive the desire to journey toward the celestial light. Though their words require repeated translation and their path spans years, they brave rugged wilderness without hesitation, prostrating themselves to behold the radiance of Your sagely sun. Even Fotucheng, who entered Xia from the east of Khotan, or Kumarajiva, who followed the Qin from the north of Kucha, cannot surpass their arduous devotion. From the depths of a subject’s heart, this devotion arises solely from the inspiration of Your sagely brilliance. May this be forever inscribed in the national annals, amplifying Your sacred achievements.

Your servant, basking in the celestial light, is overwhelmed with gratitude.

**Memorial Presenting a Portrait of the Primordial Heavenly Worthy and Merit Record for the Longevity Festival**

Your servant humbly observes that the nine bends of the limpid river and the harmonious union of heaven and earth herald omens of flowing rainbows from starry islets and flying lightning from the Dipper’s pivot. Auspicious signs align with millennia of peace, and joy pervades the myriad states.

Your Majesty, grasping the celestial tally and receiving the Mandate, presides over the realm with upright authority. You propagate the supreme Dao, surpassing the Three Sovereigns, and disseminate the highest virtue, transcending the Five Emperors. Your transformative influence permeates seas and mountains; Your grace encompasses Chinese and barbarians alike. Those clad in felt and fur regularly present tribute; the Four Wildernesses and Eight Extremities all offer precious treasures. By harmonizing the Six Treasuries, heaven bestows extraordinary omens; by penetrating the Three Springs, earth manifests wondrous gifts. All are inscribed in jade scripts—golden carp leap through waves, frost-white beasts appear, snow-winged birds soar, sacred fungi and mushrooms burgeon, and fragrant dew glistens. Immortals are often seen amidst misty crags; steadfast cypresses flourish anew in clouded valleys. Jade granaries overflow with annual abundance; treasures stream in like rivers. No one is left destitute, and every household merits enfeoffment.

Thus, distant lands admire Your sagacity, and foreign realms submit to Your court. With joyful reverence, they celebrate Your transformative influence. From the Sanggan to the vast deserts, monks like Fazheng bow in homage to heaven; from Sindhu to Jibin, the Three Treasures of Buddhism offer tribute with sincere devotion. All gaze toward the North Star and pray for the longevity of the Southern Mountains.

Now, as the sun shines with ninefold radiance and the winds harmonize with the eight directions, the grand Longevity Festival of the flourishing spring arrives, marking Your sacred and prosperous birthday. I have reverently painted a portrait of the Primordial Heavenly Worthy, wishing to enhance Your sagely blessings. Together with the Daoist assembly of this abbey, I have established a seven-day and seven-night *Lingbao* Longevity Ritual beginning on the first day of this month, with pure incense, lamps, and devout recitations. May the efficacy of the wondrous Dao eternally secure Your boundless longevity.

I humbly present the aforementioned portrait and merit record, presuming to lay them before Your celestial wisdom.

**Memorial Thanking for the Bestowal of Purple Robes upon Lü Yanchang of Yangping Mountain**

Your servant has received the imperial decree bestowing purple robes upon Lü Yanchang, Master of Yangping Mountain, and appointing him as a Great Virtue for inner palace rituals. Your grace descends from the heavens, bestowing honor upon the mountain forests. Plants and trees radiate splendor; mist and clouds shimmer with color. All who dwell in these sacred precincts, whether robed in caps or coarse garments, share in the joy of this illustrious favor.

Your servant offers his profound gratitude. Your Majesty, with sagely wisdom, inaugurated the era and grasped the celestial tally to govern the realm. Your benevolence extends across the Nine Lands, bestowing blessings upon all; Your governance spreads to the Eight Wildernesses, perfecting the harmony of a flourishing age. Thus, all regions present tribute, and interpreters from distant lands attend the court.

At this propitious moment of celebrating the imperial longevity, marking the grand festival of the season of renewal, Your Majesty’s boundless grace extends to both teachings, showering imperial favor across the ten thousand regions. Lü Yanchang has long dwelled amidst mist and clouds, refining his skill in medicinal arts. Though he devoted himself solely to cultivation and repair, he dared not aspire to such honor and glory. Yet Your Majesty, mindful of meritorious ministers, deeply commended his mastery of the healing arts. When Lü Yanchang’s prescriptions achieved remarkable efficacy, saving the life of Yan Yin—whose grave illness was thus dispelled—You bestowed upon him the highest grace, publicly conferring the robes of office. Arrayed in rainbow-hued vestments and bearing the ivory tablet, he finds the debt of heaven and earth’s favor impossible to repay; with evening candles and morning incense, he vows to answer the radiance of Your sagely illumination. Your servant and the Daoist assembly are overwhelmed.

*End of Volume Two of the Guangcheng Collection*

*Volume Three of the Guangcheng Collection*
*Composed by Du Guangting, Inner Court Attendant for Literary Compositions by Imperial Command, Great Virtue of the Upper Capital Taiqing Palace, and Recipient of the Purple Robe*

**Memorial Presenting a Twenty-Couplet Poem on the Arrival of Indian Monks**

Your servant observes that the three *samanta*s from the Western Heaven have arrived at court to pay homage. They have traversed jade passes to the north and crossed golden rivers to the west, their journey spanning layered frontiers and exceeding ten thousand *li*. Even Ban Chao’s expeditions reached only as far as Wusun, and Zhang Qian’s explorations extended no farther than Qinghai. Some paths wind through serpent-haunted deserts where human footprints vanish; others cross flying snow and shifting sands where horses’ hooves cannot tread. Thus, the reach of civilization has differed, and tribute from these lands has seldom been offered. Yet the white jade rings from Kunlun’s peaks first heralded auspicious omens, and the fiery jewels of Mount Zhong marked wondrous treasures. How much more so for those from Shendu, dwelling in the shadow of the Congling Mountains, or from Khotan, beyond the snow-crowned peaks—let alone the distant lands of India, whose arduous journey reflects their reverence. They admire the majesty of China’s myriad people and turn toward the sagely rule of Great Shu’s enlightened sovereign. Their single-minded devotion to paying homage is truly laudable in the annals of history.

Your Majesty, whose sagely essence embodies the heavens, has received the mandate to inaugurate an era. Your virtue surpasses that of Fuxi and Zhuanxu; Your benevolence eclipses that of Yao and Tang. Through civil virtue, You govern the remote frontiers; through martial prowess, You pacify the seas and lands. Thus, the western tribes submit in allegiance, and all under heaven acknowledge their rightful lord. To the south, the lands of Jiaozhi are connected; to the north, the peoples of the yurts are gathered. Tribute and offerings arrive without fail, year after year.

In the intervals of governance, You bestow blessings from the heavens, promoting and honoring both the Daoist and Buddhist teachings. Monasteries stand resplendent in their purity; Daoist temples gleam in their splendor. With unified devotion, both traditions flourish. The immortals of the Purple Cloud Grotto manifest auspicious signs, while the foreign monks of India present tribute—all drawn by Your sagely influence to bless the imperial realm. The ministers of the land and the officials of the court share in the joy, dancing in celebration.

Your servant, a humble scholar of the mushroom fields and a solitary wanderer of the clouded peaks, has been graced by Your celestial kindness to proclaim this luminous decree. With reverence, I have composed a twenty-couplet poem in seven-character lines in praise of Your sagely virtue and now present it, daring to intrude upon Your imperial majesty. I am overwhelmed with awe and trepidation.

**Memorial Congratulating the Enfeoffment of Prince Zi as Prince Zhong**

The imperial rescript descends in radiant splendor, and rituals proceed with illustrious clarity. The ancestral temple bestows felicity, while the realm rejoices in exultation.

With reverence, I offer my congratulations. May it please Your Imperial Majesty, whose benevolence extends boundless love and whose Dao cherishes steadfast renewal. You prolong the jade calendar to perpetuate prosperity and fortify the jasper branches for enduring greatness. The phoenix-script confers mandate, and the unicorn’s hooves add luster. Joyous qi ascends to the crimson heavens, while glory gathers at the vermilion palace.

Your servant, blessed to witness this sagely era and gaze upon Your majestic presence, is overwhelmed with awe.

**Memorial Congratulating the Naming of the Newly Constructed Tianxi Hall**
Your servant prostrates to acknowledge the imperial decree bestowing the name *Tianxi Hall* upon the newly completed palace within the Great Interior. The august residence is renewed, and a resplendent name is graciously conferred. Both within and beyond the realm, all rejoice in admiration, while Hua and Yi alike exult.

With reverence, I offer my congratulations. May it please Your Imperial Majesty, who holds the pivot of governance and wields the Dipper to extend the hem of Your robe. You encompass the nine lands in sovereign rule and open the four gates to foster harmony. Modeling the heavens in construction, You elevate the imperial abode in the capital; spanning the earth in foundation, You fortify the royal residence for myriad generations. Thus, the gates of the Vermilion Phoenix stretch afar, and the Dragon Court expands in grandeur. Gathering the pure radiance of sun and moon, its towering gates stand majestic; assembling the auspicious hues of stars and constellations, its literary halls open wide. Lofty and towering, it presses upon the realms of Shen and Jing; soaring and precipitous, it mirrors the forms of Di and Fang. None but that mountain spirits flew boulders, river lords contributed timber, men came forth as sons to labor, and divine aid lent its strength. Though the palaces of Hao and Lu were refined, they pale in comparison; though the halls of Han and Zhou were grand, they cannot rival this. Now that the work is complete, a precious plaque is newly bestowed. The divine is revealed by the Supreme Mystery, aligning with the Celestial Bestowal; the vast design shines to the eight extremities, eternally proclaiming Your sagely achievement. Here, You survey the seas and mountains to inspect treasures, and assemble the feudal lords to receive the homage of all nations. Great rites shall be performed to bless the myriad regions. May the divine and luminous assist in this era, and may the longevity of heaven and earth be extended.

Your servant, honored to bask in this sagely light and gaze upon this divine work, is overwhelmed with awe.

**Memorial Congratulating the Gradual Recovery of the Sacred Body**
Your servant humbly reports that, since yesterday, the Sacred Body has swiftly returned to peace and recovery. Your servant is filled with boundless joy and exultation, bowing his head again and again.

With reverence, I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty, whose profound benevolence governs the realm and whose supreme Dao extends like the hem of a robe. Grace blankets the ten thousand regions, and favor encompasses all beings. Day and night, You toil with vigilance, Your labor straining the harmony of sinews and skin; from dawn to dusk, You don robes and attend to affairs, Your concern spanning the shifts of cold and warmth. Now, the numinous and unseen assist, mountains and rivers offer their efficacy, the ancestral temple bestows auspices, and the Dark Vault descends blessings. The Sacred Rest is restored, further enhancing the brilliance of rain and sunlight; vast felicity is embraced, perpetuating the longevity of ten thousand years. Hua and Yi rejoice in delight, and the myriad peoples raise a chorus of joy.

Your servant, afflicted with an eye ailment for over ten days, has been unable to hasten to the jade palace, dance upon the celestial steps, or gaze toward the misty heavens. I am overwhelmed with awe and trepidation.

**Memorial Congratulating the Recovery from Illness**
Your servant humbly reports that the Sacred Body has fully recovered, and all ministers within and beyond the realm leap for joy. Your servant is filled with boundless exultation, bowing his head again and again.

I have heard that even the five planets in their celestial courses may deviate in motion, and the four seasons in their cycles may falter in their transitions of cold and warmth. Though the discord of cold and heat may arise, it is but the natural order of yin and yang. With reverence, I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty, who governs in accord with the seasons and rules with virtue. The myriad affairs weigh upon Your imperial heart, and the six qi occasionally disrupt the Sacred Body. Now, the divine and numinous align in assistance, the ancestral temple bestows auspices, vast celestial blessings gather, and the Sacred Rest is swiftly restored. Thus, You inherit the unified rule of Tang Yao and extend the distant longevity of Zhou’s emperors. Rewards are bestowed upon the physicians for their skill, and grace flows throughout the realm; drums resound for all beings, and their echoes shake the layered heavens.

Your servant, since the third month, has been afflicted with illness and unable to join the dance upon the steps of Yao, overwhelmed with joy and trepidation.

**Memorial Expressing Gratitude for the Imperial Edict**
Your servant humbly reports that today, I received the imperial edict bestowing a personal decree in reward for my memorial of the eleventh of this month, congratulating the recovery of the Sacred Body. Grace descends from the imperial throne, and purple seals convey favor. I look up to the celestial mandate and am humbled by the imperial consolation.

Your servant, though coarse and rustic, is fortunate to stand among the ranks. Though I daily pray for the Dragon Diagram in my devotions, I should hasten morning and night to the Phoenix Gate. Yet, afflicted by illness, I have been absent from court. Yesterday, learning that Your Imperial Majesty, burdened by the myriad affairs of state, had briefly fallen ill but swiftly recovered, I bowed my head in joy and dispatched a memorial in celebration. Such is the humble duty of one in my position, a routine observance of the ranks. Never did I expect the imperial grace to bestow this purple edict. I have reverently burned incense and knelt to receive it, overwhelmed by the sight of heaven and the weight of Your sagely favor.

**Memorial Expressing Gratitude for the Bestowal of Funds for the Daoist Ritual**
Your servant humbly reports that today, I received the imperial decree bestowing twenty strings of cash from the imperial treasury for the Daoist ritual held at the Three Clarities Altar in this abbey since the twenty-first of last month. There, the elder masters and Daoist assembly gathered to perform the *Lingbao* scripture recitation and disaster-dispelling rites for Your Imperial Majesty.

From the central court, favor is bestowed; from the inner treasury, wealth is granted. I look up to the celestial kindness and inscribe this humble gratitude in my heart.

**Memorial Expressing Gratitude for the Bestowal of Funds**
Your servant humbly prostrates in gratitude. As one presumptuously entrusted with the role of teaching master, I have deeply received the nation’s grace. All daily rites and devotions are but the fulfillment of my duty. Never did I expect Your sagely favor to descend as private beneficence. Gazing upon the dragon countenance of heaven’s Son, my awe for Your sagely virtue redoubles; cradling the imperial treasury’s *e-yan* coins, my prayers for Your longevity grow ever more fervent. The funds bestowed have been received in full with reverent kneeling and distributed to the Daoist assembly. Your servant and the Daoist community are overwhelmed with gratitude, trembling with devotion.

---

**Memorial Congratulating the Heir’s Ascension to the Throne**
Your servant reports that today, the imperial heir has assumed the precious throne, illuminating the grand enterprise. The realm rejoices, and all under heaven exults. Your servant offers his congratulations.

I have heard that when King Cheng succeeded to the throne, he upheld the illustrious governance of a thousand generations; when Emperor Shun inherited the mandate, he became the model for a hundred kings. Above, he accorded with heaven’s decree; below, he harmonized with the people’s will. Now, I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: Your Dao rivals that of Tang, Your benevolence equals that of Yu. Your virtue aligns with the five planets, Your destiny resonates with the two poles. Thus, You have worthily inherited the ancestral legacy and gloriously ascended the precious throne. The imperial mandate shines with renewal, the grand foundation heralds an era of enduring prosperity. May the realm be unified in script and axle, the Chinese and barbarians dwell in peace. May the nine lands see horses return to the mountains, the four seas know no whales crossing their expanse. May the imperial order be upheld, the great enterprise forever secure.

Your servant, honored by this flourishing era, has been counted among the court’s ranks. Though I strive to emulate the sun-bearing devotion of the loyal, my joy is but that of a turtle’s dance; though I harbor the regret of one who once lay by the Zhang River, I cannot match the swift flight of the wild duck. I am overwhelmed with reverence, leaping with devotion.

---

**Memorial Congratulating the Proclamation of a Virtuous Decree**
Your servant reports that today, the Emperor ascended the throne to proclaim a virtuous decree. I have heard that sagely virtue emulates heaven, its timely governance ever attuned to nurturing life; divine merit embodies the Dao, its seasonal blessings fostering growth. None are untouched by its grace—from the nine tribes to the myriad states, all under heaven’s cover and earth’s bearing rejoice as one.

Your servant offers his congratulations. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: enthroned at the center of the realm, Your gaze spans all under heaven. You practice frugality, leaving the thatched eaves untrimmed; You cultivate the spirit, holding the golden mirror aloft. Thus, the distant frontiers of Yan and the barren wastes beyond submit tribute like clouds; the remote lands of Jilin and the ends of the earth gather like mist, their ships and ladders converging. Your rule rests in non-action, and the people delight in the Dao.

Now, You broadly proclaim virtuous teachings, aligning with the true yang. You pacify the remnant peoples beyond the borders, raising them to a realm of longevity; You ascend the newly built hall of heavenly bestowal, fanning the fragrant winds. You console the toil of frontier soldiers, remit the arrears of taxes in prefectures and counties. Exiles and banished officials alike receive the grace of pardon; prisoners in fetters are all embraced by the lenient and enlightened statutes. Through the threefold amnesty, all shall be as one.

Your servant, bound by illness, cannot join the ranks to dance upon the jade steps. I am overwhelmed with joy, leaping with devotion.

---

**Another Memorial Congratulating the Proclamation of a Virtuous Decree**
Your servant reports that today, the Emperor ascended the throne to proclaim a virtuous decree. Thunder and rain dissolve the drought, abundant blessings flow without end, ensuring no land is left untouched and all living beings dwell in peace. The multitudes of Hua and Yi, the countless millions—who does not rejoice?

Your servant offers his congratulations. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: inheriting sagacity and continuing enlightenment, You grasp the charts and rule the realm. Your filial piety, vast as steam rising, rivals that of Emperor Hui of Han in upholding the ancestral temple; Your reverence, meticulous and humble, equals that of King Cheng of Zhou in ascending the throne. In civil matters, You cherish distant customs; in martial affairs, You pacify remote frontiers. Embracing the *qian* hexagram, Your transformative influence knows no bounds; emerging from the *zhen* hexagram, Your benevolence is complete and unbroken.

Now, You govern with serene majesty, proclaiming grace from the central hall. You pacify the people beyond the borders, raising them to a realm of longevity; You shower the realm with heavenly virtue, fanning the fragrant winds. Moved by the hardships of conscripted soldiers, You release the arrears of taxes and levies. Exiles and prisoners alike receive the private grace of amnesty, all benefiting from the lenient and enlightened statutes. Joyful voices resound beyond the borders, jubilant spirits float among the clouds. May the realm be unified in axle and script, awaiting the return to oneness. May the jade charts and celestial calendars endure for a thousand springs.

Your servant, though aged and infirm, has personally witnessed this sagely reign. Yet, afflicted by illness, I cannot dance upon the steps of Yao. Gazing longingly at Your heavenly kindness, I am overwhelmed with joy, leaping with devotion.

---

**Memorial Expressing Gratitude for the Imperial Response**
Your servant reports that I have received the imperial rescript, which graciously responded to my memorial of the second day of this month congratulating Your accession to the throne. Favor descends from the vermilion heavens, bestowing honor upon the Daoist teachings. The five-colored imperial edict emerges from the immortal precincts, resplendent; the nine-rayed sun shines upon the fields of magic mushrooms, luminous.

Overwhelmed by this honor, I am at a loss, my joy boundless. Your servant humbly prostrates in gratitude. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: the pearl balance brings forth auspicious omens, the jade dipper unfurls divine power. Emerging from the *zhen* domain, You renew the light; inheriting the *qian* pivot, You ascend as the sagely heir. Your virtue surpasses that of the ancient sages, Your filial piety vast as You govern with folded arms; Your brilliance continues the illustrious legacy, Your great luminosity reigning over the realm. Profound grace spreads afar, abundant blessings extend everywhere. Joyful voices shake the earth like thunder, jubilant spirits condense in the sky like a canopy. The multitudes of Hua and Yi turn toward the sun, gazing at the clouds.

Your servant, constrained by age and affliction, cannot approach the dragon steps to present my pure devotion or join the ranks in the beast dance. Yet, I offered my sealed memorial from afar, humbly expressing my sincerity. Never did I expect such exalted praise, the imperial rescript descending like heavenly script. The auspicious dew of virtuous conduct glistens, the fragrant clouds of imperial favor gather. Holding the response, I feel the weight of Mount Song and Mount Heng insufficient; moved by grace, I find the depths of the four seas inadequate. Though as insignificant as the wren, I cannot repay the boundless heavens and earth.

The imperial rescript bestowed has been reverently received with incense and kneeling. I am overwhelmed with gratitude, bearing the sagely favor.

---

**Memorial Requesting the Imperial Edict for the Major Mourning Rites**
Your servant kowtows repeatedly. Time passes unceasingly, and the late Emperor has now reached the major mourning rites. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: in grief and longing, Your sagely heart is inconsolable. Above, You honor the ancestral temple; below, You comply with the will of the countless. By observing the great rites, You forever bless the Hua and Yi.

Your servant, bound by age and illness, cannot join the ranks to offer condolences.

Your servant is overwhelmed with grief, prostrate and trembling beyond measure. I humbly submit this memorial to offer condolences.

**Memorial on the Release from Mourning Attire**
Your servant kowtows repeatedly. Time passes unceasingly, and the late Emperor’s passing seems but yesterday, now having completed the rites of mourning. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: in eternal longing and grief, Your sagely heart is inconsolable. The four seas and all subjects have fulfilled the mourning rites. Gazing at the heavens, I am left helpless; treading the earth, I find no place for myself. Your servant, bound by age and illness, cannot hasten to the palace to express my sorrow. I am overwhelmed with choking grief and longing beyond measure. I humbly submit this memorial to offer condolences.

**Memorial on the Bestowal of the Temple Name and Posthumous Title**
Your servant states: On this day of the present month, the late Emperor’s exalted posthumous title and temple name have been conferred. I reflect upon the late Emperor: born in response to Heaven’s mandate, he rode the tide of destiny to unfold his great enterprise. His robes, grand as those of Feng and Pei, surpassed the merits of the Han founder; his virtue, like the branches of Bin and Qi, exceeded the benevolence of King Wen of Zhou. He embodied the name of Tang Yao, who aided the virtuous, and followed the illustrious title of Yu Shun, whose brilliance shone forth. Now, as we honor his exalted posthumous title, we extol his sagely achievements. All within the realm grieve as one, moved by shared sorrow. I reflect upon Your Majesty: boundless in grief, You govern with filial piety. Gazing upon the imperial regalia, You find no solace; receiving the decree, Your sorrow deepens. All under heaven share in this profound mourning.

**Memorial on the Opening of the Temporary Palace**
Your servant states: I have learned that on this day of the present month, the temporary palace of the late Emperor has been opened. Princes and ministers are wrapped in sorrow; the six palaces resound with wailing. I reflect upon Your Majesty: in grief and longing, Your sagely heart is inconsolable. Facing the imperial regalia, Your sorrow grows; reflecting on the fleeting light, You are lost in mourning. Your servant, bound by age and illness, cannot join the ranks in lamentation. I am overwhelmed with grief, prostrate and trembling beyond measure.

**Memorial on the Completion of the Ancestral Temple Rites**
Your servant kowtows repeatedly. I have learned that the rites for the late Emperor’s enshrinement in the ancestral temple have been completed. The rites honor the ancestral sacrifices, and the order of generations is duly observed. By upholding the solemn ceremonies, the divine merits shine forth. I reflect upon Your Majesty: in reverence for the ritual classics and devotion to filial virtue, You have established the proper rites of spring and autumn sacrifices, and the grand ceremonies of offering to Heaven and serving the ancestors. May these great blessings forever grace the sacred temple. All under heaven share in this profound mourning and longing.

**Memorial on the Naming of the Imperial Mausoleum**
Your servant kowtows repeatedly. I have witnessed the late Emperor’s mausoleum being named [X] Mausoleum. I reflect upon the late Emperor: his birth was marked by auspicious omens, his reign guided by celestial signs. Grasping the primal *qi* of Heaven, he inaugurated his dynasty; expanding the wilds of Earth, he laid its foundations. He disdained the trifling divisions of Wu and Wei, extending his transformative grace; aspiring to unify Hua and Yi, he sought to harmonize all under one rule. The naming of his mausoleum fittingly accords with his sagely virtue. I reflect upon Your Majesty: inheriting the weighty duty of succession, You honor the past while advancing the legacy. Illuminating his enduring merits, You enhance the splendor of these grand rites. Gazing upon his virtuous footsteps, Your sagely heart finds slight solace. All ministers share in this profound sorrow and longing.

**Memorial on the Procession of the Imperial Funeral Cortege**
Your servant states: I reflect upon the late Emperor’s spirit chariot, which sets forth on this day of the present month. Heaven and Earth mingle in sorrow; sun and moon lose their light. All subjects grieve as one; clouds and mist darken in mourning. Your servant is crushed with grief, choking with sorrow, and kowtows repeatedly. I reflect upon Your Majesty: Your filial devotion knows no bounds, and Your sagely heart is inconsolable. As the divine chariot grows ever more distant, the sound of the funeral dirge deepens Your sorrow. In ceaseless longing, Your lamentation is unbearable.

**Memorial Congratulating the Emperor on Resuming Court Audience After Ascension**
Your servant states: I have learned that on the ninth day of this month, the Emperor ascended the Mingde Hall to hold court. The regalia and banners were first arrayed upon the jade steps; the ranks of officials, like soaring cranes and egrets, stood in formation upon the jeweled terrace.

The realm rejoices as one, and the world celebrates in unison. Your servant is filled with boundless joy and leaps with exultation, kowtowing repeatedly. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: born of the Nine Heavens, Your sagely might governs the Seven Celestial Luminaries. Grasping the jade Dipper, You guide the celestial dragon to bring peace to the Four Seas; holding the jade sighting-tube, You oversee the great cosmos to shepherd the myriad regions. You have unfolded the civil brilliance of the ancient sage-kings and cultivated the virtue and power of the former monarchs. Now, the clouds part to reveal the azure vault, and all revere the Pole Star’s majesty; the mists disperse over the boundless sea, and all pay homage to the radiance of the Great Luminance. Your grace extends without limit, and Your benevolence flows without end. Though I, Your servant, remain distant in the fields of immortals, I am honored to witness this auspicious era. Moved by sorrowful verses, I grieve my inability to hasten to the Han palace. Gazing toward the sky of Yao, I cannot contain my exultant joy, my fervent delight, my overwhelming emotion.

**Memorial Offering Consolation Upon the Completion of the Imperial Mausoleum**
Your servant states: I have learned that the rites for the mausoleum of the Late Emperor are now complete. The divine palace is sealed forever, and the immortal chamber rests in eternal peace. All within the realm, unable to bear their lamentation, grieve as one. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: Your longing knows no respite, and Your sagely heart is inconsolable. Facing the grave mound, sorrow deepens; grasping the dragon’s whiskers, Your grief is everlasting. The traveling robes remain, yet the divine chariot has long since departed. Recalling His majesty and might, my sorrow and longing are beyond measure. Your servant, confined by frailty and illness, cannot attend to offer consolation at the palace gates. I am overwhelmed with grief, choking with sorrow.

**Memorial Requesting Permission Not to Attend the Imperial Mausoleum**
Your servant states: I have learned that the mausoleum is near completion, and Your Imperial Majesty, in boundless grief and longing, wishes to attend the tomb in person. I have reverently heard the imperial decree, and it has struck terror into the hearts of all. Every subject under Your radiance is filled with dread and confusion. Your servant is truly alarmed and fearful, kowtowing repeatedly. I humbly consider: the filial piety of emperors and kings follows Heaven, accords with the people, and adheres to principle in establishing rites, ensuring that all living beings conform and the ancestral temples remain eternally secure. Never has it been heard that one should express filial devotion through the sorrow of bow and sword or emulate the solitary conduct of Zeng and Min. To suddenly mobilize the imperial guard and personally oversee the rites would be unprecedented. I reflect upon Your Imperial Majesty: examining the ancient rituals of the hundred kings and adhering to the established precedents of successive dynasties, may You turn Your sagely gaze and align with the principles of ritual propriety. By following the universal norms of antiquity, You will set a model for future rulers, further manifesting the principles of filial governance and consoling the realm. Your servant, unable to contain his earnest and fervent plea, respectfully presents this memorial to make his request known.

*End of Volume Three of the* Guangcheng Collection
*Volume Four of the* Guangcheng Collection *begins*

The Most Reverend Du Guangting, Grand Master of Imperial Compositions, Purple-Robed Virtue of the Supreme Clarity Palace in the Upper Capital, has composed the *Ritual Petition for the Promotion and Deliverance of the Perfected* on behalf of Minister of Revenue, Duke Zhang, for the advancement of the departed.

Your servant has learned that the Supreme One unfolded the sacred diagrams, and the Primordial Sovereign expounded the teachings. The Three Registers established the golden and luminous canons, their merit extending to humans and heavens; the Nine Dark Realms suspended the jade tablets of ordinances, their grace encompassing the living and the dead. Tracing the purport of the scriptures and adhering to the mysterious texts, I humbly beseech the mercy of promotion and deliverance, and thus prepare this earnest petition of repentance.

On the twenty-fifth day of this month falls the death anniversary of my late mother, Lady Liu, Tang Dynasty Lady of Chu State, posthumously honored as Grand Lady of Song State by the Former Shu. On the thirtieth day of this month falls the death anniversary of my late father, former Tang Chancellor and Grand Preceptor to the Crown Prince, posthumously honored as Grand Commandant by the Former Shu.

With reverence, I present offerings of oil, candles, incense, and alms, to be consecrated at the Northern Emperor Cloister of the Jade Bureau in Chengdu Prefecture, where a *Lingbao* *Mingzhen* ritual will be performed for one day and one night. Fourteen Daoist priests will conduct the Dao at three intervals and recite the scriptures at three intervals. Baring my heart before the celestial patterns, I dispatch the fragrant dragon to present this petition on high.

May the Most Exalted One deign to look with compassion, and may the host of sages bestow their radiance, universally notifying the Four Offices and informing the Three Realms. May the Nine Dragon Mandates descend, unlocking the cold courts of eternal night, refining and bathing the forms and souls, promoting and delivering the divine spirits. May they depart the palace of dark yin and enter the palace of cavernous yang. May transgressions and faults be absolved, grievances and enmities dissolved. May their names be stricken from the earthly registers and inscribed upon the ranks of the Dao. May they revolve toward the land of blessings and ascend to the ranks of immortals. May the ninefold dark consciousnesses all attain transcendence.

I vow to cultivate devotion with diligence, repaying the grace of the true numina above.

*Ritual Petition for the Yellow Register Retreat at the Residence of the Grand Lady of the Zhang Clan*

I reflect that the wondrous Dao and its mysterious efficacy aid the times and assist the state. The true scriptures and their secret purport rescue beings and save humanity.

At the inception of the cosmic order, ere the passage of countless kalpas, the vast transformation of the Dao unfolded across the ten thousand heavens. Those who honor it store blessings and receive protection; those who cultivate it ride the radiant clouds and ascend at dawn. Through the ages, its luminous canon and sacred decrees have shone forth. The Zhang clan has inherited auspicious favor, its fortune aligned with sagely brilliance. Bathed in celestial light, they reflect the splendor of imperial grace. Mindful of their allotted portion, they ever hold reverent caution, examining themselves and ever heeding bright admonitions. Yet they fear that the accumulated blemishes of past lives remain unrepented, and the encumbrances of this existence may deepen. In the shadowy yin, there are registers of litigation; in the obscure void, there are ledgers of life’s reckoning.

Moreover, this year for the Zhang clan, the celestial tally descends upon the Wood Tomb position, while dark stars lodge in the year of Flying Transformation. Mars shines upon the Palace of Self, still clashing with their inherent nature. The great fortune meets the ascendant Metal, its fire power somewhat diminished; the minor fortune resides in the realm of generating Metal, its Wood qi already attenuated. Reflecting upon this convergence of adversities, their anxiety redoubles. Yet the boundless Dao knows no limit in bestowing grace universally. Thus, with earnest devotion, they offer prayers, assured of receiving blessings and felicity. Therefore, they purify their cinnabar hearts and undertake the Yellow Register Retreat. Arraying the ritual in solemn ranks before the jade altar, they unfold its sacred contents. Presenting their sincerity to the myriad heavens, they kindle orchid lamps through the midnight hours; proclaiming their vows to the Three Realms, they waft sandalwood and orchid incense through the nine watches. With earnest supplication, they beseech mercy and repentance.

They humbly implore the Most High and the myriad sages and perfected ones to look upon their prayers with compassion and manifest their abundant grace. May they command the celestial and terrestrial bureaus, the yin officials and yang offices, to strike their names from the black registers and inscribe them in the azure palace. May debts and litigations be harmonized, grievances and enmities dissolved. May the Northern Capital remove the records of confrontation and deception, extending their years; may the Southern Culmen fix the tally of prolonged life, ensuring prosperity and longevity. May the Five Phases dispel the texts of disaster and stagnation, and the Nine Luminaries cease their baleful influences. May they ever rejoice in the sunlit days of Shun and forever thrive under the heavens of Yao. May their kin enjoy peace and well-being, their descendants loyalty and filial piety. May the ninefold dark consciousnesses and the seven generations of ancestors, along with all departed forebears—whether bound in the gloomy thoroughfares or yet to ascend the path of blessings—by the power of the Dao swiftly attain rebirth. May the living receive blessings and assuredly meet with true felicity. May all beings in the three paths and six destinies, dwelling in the cold realms of the night, through the bond of repentance and purification, fully attain the fruit of liberation. May the yin and yang officers, the dragon spirits of the residence, long delight in tranquility, and may misfortune and decline be extinguished.

Above all, may the imperial domain expand afar, the sagely lifespan extend boundlessly. May its years surpass those of the Zhou, its prosperity exceed that of the Han. May the world be unified, its scripts and chariot-tracks harmonized. May all hearts turn toward the sun with reverence, and all bathe in the blessings bestowed from heaven.

*Ritual Petition for the Yellow Register Retreat by the Attendant for Ritual Protection and Blessing*

I have heard that the Dao, in its fundamental non-action, descends primordial essence to generate the Two Modes; from these modes arise numbers, which array the Five Wefts and complete the myriad forms. Earth aligns with heaven, never deviating from the celestial patterns; yang expands and yin contracts, all dependent upon their regulation. Thus, good and evil cycle endlessly, fortune and misfortune lie in wait. The firmness of Qian and the receptivity of Kun cannot avert the appointed times of nine and six; the moon’s orb and the sun’s wheel cannot alter the waxing and waning of their phases. How much more so for the two poles, endowed with their natures, and the three destinies, fixed at birth? Before transcending the mechanism of transformation, they are inherently subject to the principle of change. Therefore, one should ever hold caution in the heart, examine faults and recognize errors. Constantly rousing oneself with diligent effort, one may hope to move the gaze of the true numina.

Your servant has long received the shade of the mysterious, early bathed in abundant favor. My fortune has aligned with sagely brilliance, and I have presumptuously received esteemed appointment. Though I have striven to offer loyal service, my efforts to aid and succor remain unfulfilled; though I have supported the sagely and upheld heaven, I have repeatedly received surpassing grace. Entrusted with the seal of the altar and the insignia of office, my commission has grown ever more exalted. Leading the army with the green sash, my honors have deepened. Yet I fear that in fullness lies peril, and how may I repay the sovereign and father? I still dread that in action and stillness, I may fall short of my allotted portion; in thought and deed, I may offend the divine. Perhaps in public affairs, I have erred in rewards and punishments; in leading the multitude, I have faltered in judgment. Or perhaps the transgressions of past lives remain unresolved, or the karmic debts of accumulated lives unremoved. Any such failing must be repented and purified.

Moreover, this year, both major and minor fortunes converge upon the Tomb position, while the Flying Palace still encounters Mars. Though I reside in the direction of the Flowery Canopy, where fortune and virtue abide, I fear the baleful influences of punishment and conflict. With such trepidation, my earnest sincerity redoubles. In the midst of the Xu clan’s yearly fortunes, there are also stagnations. Both major and minor fortunes see the Metal and Fire qi diminished; the Flying Palace meets Ketu, and the celestial tally descends upon the birth month. Fearing these portents of disaster and stagnation, I am resolved to repent and pray. Thus, I reverently prepare the tokens of sincerity and devoutly undertake the retreat. Following the standards of the Mysterious Capital, I establish the Yellow Register ritual arena. For two days and six watches, I array fragrant flowers and summon the true sages from all heavens and earths. Concentrating spirit and fixing intent, I pour forth my earnest supplication.

I humbly implore the myriad sages to turn their light and the host of perfected ones to bestow their gaze, moved by my sincere devotion to grant blessings and felicity. May they absolve the sins and blemishes of the past and dispel the adversities to come. May the bright stars and dark luminaries bring no baleful influences; may the Three Destinies and Five Phases remove the clashes and obstacles. May grievances be harmonized, litigations dissolved. May descendants flourish, longevity and prosperity increase. May the ninefold dark consciousnesses receive blessings, the gloom of night be illuminated. May kin enjoy peace, dragon spirits rest in contentment. Above all, may the sagely person enjoy boundless longevity, the great enterprise ever flourish. May the voice of instruction spread to the nine regions, all rejoicing in the grace of Shun; may the scripts and chariots be unified to the eight extremities, all delighting in the benevolence of Yao. May the hundred grains abound, the six qi flow harmoniously. I vow to offer utmost loyalty and filial piety, repaying the sagely and enlightened grace; to rouse my sincerity, looking up to the protection of the true numina.

*Ritual Petition for the Yellow Register Retreat by Shangguan Zirong*

I reflect that the vast power of the Dao and its wondrous efficacy, the utmost truth and mysterious resonance, flow blessings according to circumstance and extend mercy in response to prayers. Aiding the state and saving the people, their grace encompasses all beings; dispelling disaster and bestowing fortune, their kindness reaches both the manifest and the hidden.

All petitions here raised shall surely receive luminous scrutiny. The petitioner, [Name] Clan, fears that within the cycles of major and minor fate this year, the Three Lifespans may wane; amid the configurations of yin-yang and celestial lodgings, the Five Planets may exert baleful influence. Thus disaster and misfortune arise, with no recourse for supplication. Having heard of the wondrous efficacy of the Yellow Register Retreat—its merit vast, its power dissolving all calamities and averting all misfortunes—I pour forth my sincerity, hoping to receive the mysterious protection. Reverently following the ritual statutes, I establish the altar precinct: three days of incense and lamps, nine intervals of repentance and thanksgiving. The utmost truth responds in hidden ways, and every entreaty finds its answer. I humbly pray that the Three Realms’ heavens, the lofty perfected, and the host of sages descend boundless grace and extend the sheltering favor of broad coverage. For the [Name] Clan, may they dissolve accumulated transgressions of past lives and debts of enmity from many rebirths. As repentance is offered, may they be smoothed away; as the hour arrives, may they be swept clean. May kinfolk dwell in peace and stability, public and private affairs flourish in harmony. I vow to offer utmost loyalty and filial piety, forever upholding the sagely mandate.

*Ritual Petition for the Yellow Register Retreat by Feilong Tangyi, Minister of the Secretariat*

I have heard that in the primordial stillness, at the origin of the undifferentiated, the Dao gave birth to the primal qi, which divided into the Two Modes. Yin and yang differ in ascent and descent; purity and turbidity distinguish immortals from mortals. Thus the Purple Clarity’s golden gates stand high in the court of supreme mystery, while the Yellow Axis’ wind barrier guards the nethermost depths. As beings are stained by delusion, doubts of advance and retreat arise; as they drift in sinking and floating, the pain of dispersal follows. Lacking prior awakening, they must rely on guidance. The August Lord of the Dao, in the final years of the Eastern Han, opened the treasure canon of the Southern Palace, first transmitting the true registers to greatly deliver all beings. Those who cultivate it ride the clouds and soar into emptiness; those who practice it aid the people and assist the state. Some quell the vapors of disorder, some chastise and reform malevolent spirits. They rectify the celestial origins of sun and moon, harmonizing wind and clouds with the seasons; they pacify disasters and perversities in the earth’s records, ensuring the growth of plants without fault. Revered through the ages, their blessings are inexhaustible. I have long received the shelter of the Dao and enjoyed the emperor’s grace. Though my merit is slight, the profound favor grows ever deeper; though my strength is weak, the debt to ruler and parents remains unpaid. I constantly aspire to receive the secret registers and honor the sacred texts, diligently tending the incense and lamps from dawn to dusk, rousing my devotion in prayer and supplication. I hope that state and family alike may receive blessings and good fortune. Now, having strictly prepared the ritual offerings, I reverently open the altar ground, repenting and purifying through the night, prostrating in homage and taking refuge. Orchid lamps illuminate the nine nether realms by night; sandalwood incense ascends to the Three Realms by morning. With earnest reverence, I send forth my plea, hoping it reaches the august numina. I humbly invoke the Most High Three Honored Ones, the August Lord of the Primordial Dao, the sages of the ten directions, and the mighty deities of the Three Caverns: may they perceive my sincere devotion and grant responsive efficacy. May the divine officials and true qi bestow transmission, enabling inner protection of bodily peace and outer resolution of disasters and obstacles. May my name be entered in the registers of the Dao, my sins erased in the courts of darkness. May the Nine Mysteries depart the realm of accumulated night, forever dwelling in eternal joy; may the entire clan enjoy boundless goodness, ever serving the radiant and luminous. May lifespan extend far, public and private affairs know purity and prosperity. Above, I pray that the dragon charts endure long, the phoenix calendar extend in grandeur. May the sagely lifespan increase without limit, heaven and earth share eternal duration; may imperial grace spread to all bounds, seas and mountains know peace. Together may we embody the wind of the utmost Dao, jointly flourish in the transformation of non-action.

*Ritual Petition for the Retreat at Mount Qingcheng by the Crown Prince*

I have heard that the rules of the Numinous Treasure, through fasting and purification, evoke the signs of the subtle and formless; the sacred texts establish teachings, linking conduct and concealment to the work of cultivation. All begin in the heart and expand through the Dao. Above, they can reverently entreat the celestial vault, illuminating the mysterious and subtle; next, they can proclaim sincerity and extend blessings and protection. Reflecting on my pure faith, I dare to offer reverent devotion. I humbly consider that the emperor, carving out territory and establishing the foundation, models heaven in his sheltering care. He pacified chaos and inherited the virtue of earth; he elucidated truth and responded to the phase of metal. With utmost caution, he has borne the fear of treading on thin ice; with unceasing vigilance, he has endured the toil of wind and rain. Through the passing years, his reverence has only grown. Thus the land enjoys abundant harvests, the state wealth and military strength. He secured the borders of Shu and Han, controlled the strategic passes of Qian and Wu. In civil and martial arts alike, he ordered the constant norms; in utmost impartiality and fairness, he exalted the roots of governance. The four quarters admire his righteousness, the myriad lands return to his benevolence. Ships and carriages traverse no barriers of height or depth; writing and wheels align with the transforming influence. This is the shelter of the nine heavens’ numina, the hidden support of the great Dao. Thus the imperial enterprise flourishes, the celestial calculations endure. My admiration and reverence grow ever deeper, my vigilance ever more earnest. Yet with celestial signs lingering, time’s passage slightly delayed, and the observed divisions of the heavens, prayer and supplication are truly needed. Therefore, I purify my resolve and cleanse my heart, relinquishing cunning and clarifying my thoughts. I summon the ritual companions of the Ten Isles, adhere to the mysterious statutes of the Three Caverns, reverently establish the pure retreat, and proceed with the grand offering. I humbly pray that the perfected above descend their scrutiny, the host of sages proclaim their mercy. May they turn the axis at the mysterious barrier, kindle radiance on the cinnabar path. May all spoken disasters be dissolved, all auspicious signs received and answered. May the sagely lifespan increase beyond a thousand autumns, the imperial way spread through the ten thousand regions. May the mountain of longevity rise higher than the Five Peaks, the sea of fortune deeper than the Eight Seas. May it stand firm with heaven and earth, shine bright with sun and moon. May it harmonize with the sentiments of the Hua and Rong in their veneration, fulfill the earnest pleas of ministers and children. In exhausting the profound teachings, may it graciously meet my humble devotion, though I dare to disturb the true immortals. I am overwhelmed with awe and trepidation, my fervor and anxiety beyond measure. I respectfully dispatch the Great Master of Attaining Unity, Purple-Robed Zhang Maoqing, and fourteen others to reverently perform the ritual, praying that my sincere devotion be perceived.

*Ritual Petition for the Golden Register Retreat on Behalf of the Emperor by Princess Pukang*

I have heard that the Dao blends into emptiness and non-being, melting the dark and yellow to form the beginning of the Nine Mysteries; images congeal from the indistinct, marking nurturance and transformation as the sole source of creation. Thus heaven and earth cover and support, sun and moon illuminate. The Three Powers share the Dao, employing hardness and softness. As the myriad beings arise in succession, the origins of good and evil unfold, and so afterward they are ordered: rulers and fathers descend to govern, ministers and limbs assist.

The virtue of the August Thearch transcends governance, embodying the boundless warmth of the Supreme Emperor’s silent nurturance. Vastly securing the realm’s borders, broadly sheltering the black-haired people.

We humbly recall that Your Imperial Majesty, emerging from the east to govern the people, succeeds the celestial mandate. Endowed with the radiant essence of the cosmic pivot, infused with the numinous origins of mountains and rivers, Your wisdom aligns with the Three Luminaries, Your rule harmonizes with the Four Seasons. At this moment of perfect accord between heaven and humanity, prophetic omens and auspicious signs converge. Moved by the decline of former ages, You have brought peace to the multitudes, pacified the commanderies and states, and divided the rivers and mountains. Your toils equal the labors of Great Yu; Your transformative influence rivals the virtue of the Zhou. How could You forget the cares of dawn and dusk, sparing no effort in Your devotion? Thus, harmony prevails, and eternal tranquility is sought.

Now, as the season turns to the first month and the solar term meets the height of yang, when the two qi are about to merge and the fiery brilliance of the noon position blazes, we aspire to magnify a hundred blessings and offer prayers for a thousand years of longevity. We open the sacred altar of the Golden Register and ascend the sublime precincts of the Jade Capital. We humbly pray that Your Majesty’s wisdom may equal the moon’s osmanthus, Your longevity rival the celestial elm. Wielding the golden mirror to govern the realm, You bring joy to the myriad peoples with overflowing goblets. Beneath Your imperial canopy, You inquire of the Dao, beholding the loyalty of the noble ministers; from Your throne, You harmonize the primal qi, securing the assistance of the finest advisors. May the realm endure as long as the Three August Ones, and the Six Directions know no peril. Reverently serving the August Emperor of the Void, we look up to the profound workings of creation, hoping our sincere prayers be received and our earnest supplications answered.

*Ritual Petition for the Golden Register Retreat on Behalf of the Emperor by the Crown Prince*

We acknowledge that the vast and boundless Dao nurtures heaven and earth, while the unfathomable workings of the mysterious power govern creation. It condenses the primal qi to give rise to the Three Powers and pervades the Six Voids to animate the myriad beings. Thus, the spring sovereign and autumn emperor, the cloud chronicles and fire officials, wielding wondrous efficacy, govern the realm and, embodying non-action, unify heaven and earth. How could they not embrace harmony, treasuring purity and uprightness? With reverent clarity, they uphold the great image, and humanity rides the soaring dragon. Though their transformative influence melts metal and scorches stone, the virtue of Tang shines ever brighter; though floods engulfed mountains and submerged hills, the winds of Yao spread ever wider.

The Emperor, responding to the prophetic charts and assuming the throne, established the foundation. He reveres the frugal and compassionate lineage of the Mysterious Origin and follows the footsteps of the Yellow Emperor’s *Huaxu* dream. Day by day, he remains vigilant, never resting even in times of prosperity. Thus, his moral influence spreads far and wide, grain overflows the granaries, customs attain leisure and joy, and the people delight in harmony. Neighboring states exchange goodwill, and tribute pours in from the remotest lands. Deeply awed, he bears the burden of the vast heavens.

Recently, as celestial omens flared and heavenly signs issued warnings—though their paths diverged across the constellations—our prayers and supplications redoubled in earnest devotion. Reverently establishing the imperial altar, we dare to seek abundant blessings. Gazing upon the mysterious transformations of the Jade Purity, we bow our heads in reverence; opening the Daoist precinct of the Golden Register, we purify our hearts and make our vows. Our greatest wish is to convey our sincerity to the azure heavens and extend the Emperor’s longevity, that he may share the brilliance of the sun and moon and the enduring vastness of heaven and earth.

The blue-green memorial is presented, veiling the golden wisdom in radiance; the vermilion petition reaches the perfected, aligning the pearl talismans with their proper measure. May disasters and calamities forever cease, and auspicious signs perpetually arrive. May the imperial reign be harmoniously attuned, and the wolf-smoke of war never alarm. May governance surpass the Three and Five, and the imperial line extend for myriad millennia. Though I, unworthy, dwell in the Eastern Palace, I truly revere the immortal realms. Thus, I pour forth my earnest devotion, looking up to the mysterious compassion.

*Ritual Petition for the Golden Register Retreat During the Middle Prime by the Assembly*

We have heard that the supreme Dao is subtle and formless, its true essence profoundly tranquil. It extends its transformative influence beyond the primordial chaos and concentrates its radiance before the Great Ultimate. Dispersing the root of pure unity, it subtly distinguishes the steps of creation; stirring the qi of the Three Powers, it governs the realm. Thus, the sovereigns who rode dragons and inherited the qi, and those who drew the hexagrams and draped their robes, unfolded the essentials of the Dao, establishing the imperial foundation. Expanding its wondrous efficacy to bless the realm, they spread divine works to benefit all under heaven. The imperial records shine brilliantly, and human culture flourishes resplendently.

Rightly does the sagacious court correspond to this mandate, born to receive the celestial gaze. The Emperor, embodying the celestial mandate, responds to the prophetic charts. He continues the numinous lineage of the Yellow Emperor and Zhuanxu, and emulates the supreme virtue of King Wen, his royal father. Inheriting the earthly destiny, he illuminates the golden balance. His imperial canopy manifests reverent clarity, and he aspires to the true governance of Yao and Shun. He seeks to realize the great harmony and bring peace to the people of the Nine Lands. Harvests are bountiful in succession, and both Hua and Rong enjoy tranquility. The Crown Prince shines with the beauty of double brightness, and distant lands praise the winds of the Dao. Within and without, all is serene; the living beings are at peace.

Moreover, as the season of the Three Primes arrives and the great amnesty heralds an auspicious time, it is fitting to offer the sincerity of fasting and purity, jointly praying for the longevity of the sovereign and parents. Sweeping the jade altar to perform the rites, we arrange the ceremonies according to the Golden Register. With dragon-like sincerity, we prepare incense and flowers as tokens. The flames of the nine-rayed lotus lamps illuminate the dark underworld; the fragrant smoke of the three-pure sandalwood ascends to the true realms.

We earnestly hope that the Three Heavens will bestow their blessings, and the myriad sages extend their compassion, that the ancestral temples flourish and the precious charts remain secure. May the Emperor’s longevity equal heaven and earth, and his wisdom match the sun and moon. May his civil virtue and martial achievements bring peace to the Eight Extremities. May the imperial lineage shine for ten thousand years, and the Crown Prince enjoy the longevity of the camphor and osmanthus. May he ever support the great enterprise; may the empress and consorts embody the virtue of the floating duckweed and knotted cords, jointly assisting the imperial residence. May the vermilion palace and the pure court ever receive abundant blessings. May the outer domains and inner ministers increasingly tread the path of殊荣. May all constantly delight in harmony and prosperity, attaining wealth and longevity.

For those burdened by accumulated misfortunes, past debts, former enmities, or calamities of fate and destiny—afflictions from the reckoning of years, the flying banners of misfortune—we beseech that through this repentance and absolution, all be dissolved and pacified.

We further pray that the ancestral temples’ revered spirits and the Three Realms of the living deities may grant that we, our nine generations of ancestors, and the seven lineages of forebears, receive the blessings of all heavens, bestowing prosperity and transmitting boundless felicity.

May the celestial patterns shine brightly, and the celestial bodies remain pure. May the banners of the Great Unity reverse their course, and the radiance of the jade comets and golden rays cease. May anxieties be dispelled from the lands of Jing and Shen, and blessings and good fortune extend to the regions of Liang and Yi. May the Nine Grains know no peril, and the Five Weapons be sheathed.

May locusts and droughts not disrupt the farmers’ toil; may epidemics and famine not bring calamity to the villages and hamlets. May the passes and frontiers know ease and abundance, all living things flourish in their kinds; may seas and mountains return to benevolence, and the realm receive transformation.

Among those who have rendered service—generals who stood firm, commanders who have passed on, those whose merits shone in defending the throne, whose loyalty was proven in the ultimate sacrifice—whenever we offer vegetarian rites and prayers, we always include them in our repentance and supplication. May they all depart the dark and desolate realms and attain the joys of carefree wandering. Yet if some still linger in the shadows of the underworld, untouched by liberating grace, or if their descendants are gone and offerings are lacking, may the talismanic commands of the Nine Palaces swiftly guide their spirits onward. Through the vast mercy of the Three Registers, may all be delivered from suffering. Let them no longer be afflicted by illness, but hasten to the courts of blessing. May all beings—whether moving or still, flying or submerged—ascend to the true Dao.

*Emperor’s Prayer at the Auspicious Talisman Retribution and Grace Vegetarian Rite*

We have heard that emperors of successive dynasties, having received the celestial talismanic mandate, all revered the supreme Dao to govern their grand designs. None failed to govern the people with the treasure of compassion or to aid all beings through the workings of mysterious power. Thus they brought about eras of harmony and prosperity, and were granted texts of auspicious omens in return.

Now, reflecting upon our own humble self, we have undeservedly ascended the great throne. The realm remains unsettled, and though we yearn to lay down arms, peace has not yet been achieved. While decrees have been issued and laws enacted, we strive to reduce punishments but have not yet succeeded. Inwardly, we remain vigilant and diligent, never daring to rest at ease.

This year, in the seventh month, Guo Huizhi, a commoner of Shifang County in Hanzhou, while gathering herbs and tilling the land at Xianju Abbey, unearthed a bronze tablet measuring seven *cun* in length and four *cun* in width, inscribed with sixty characters. As recorded in *Laozi’s Record of Heavenly Communications*: "In the *dingmao* year, the *jiaxu* and *yihai* months, the Human King shall be born and enjoy a reign of two hundred years. The Son of Heaven shall be Wang Cong; Wang Yuanying, Wang Wanggan, Wang Yue, Wang Ze, and Wang Daoyi." Following these five characters in seal script is the inscription: "Zhang Hongdao of Beimang transformed; in the Tianbao era, this remains for a sagely age." Reverently receiving this mysterious favor, we devoutly bear the sacred talisman. Recognizing the great Dao’s bestowed blessings and foreseeing the enduring prosperity of the divined years, we prostrate ourselves in sincere devotion to repay this extraordinary grace. In accordance with the nine-grade ritual statutes, we perform the rites of the *Lingbao* scriptures. May our earnest hearts directly reach the sagely gaze. May the altars and state flourish eternally, auspicious omens surely manifest, the four seasons align in harmony, and all things thrive in abundance. May all within the realm become guests of the land, each preserving boundless fortune. We bow our heads and present this reverent petition.

*Two Hymns by Huang Qi to Assist the Zhongyuan Yellow Register Rite*
*Second Hymn: Lamp-Lighting Prayer*

We have heard that the Three Yuan’s great amnesty marks the day when the heavens descend their blessings, and the nine nights of profound darkness are the realm where the earth’s dense yin prevails. To dispel accumulated shadows, we rely upon the divine lamps. Above, they receive the light of the Three Luminaries; below, they illuminate all beings. As the scriptures and rituals esteem, salvation and protection take precedence. Now, as the season arrives at the Zhongyuan altar, we open the Yellow Register’s threefold morning repentance, dissolving ten thousand sins. We prepare fragrant oil to jointly offer this devotion. May the radiance of phoenix flames coalesce within the earthly prisons, and starlight unfold like lotuses, scattering brilliance within the gates of the Yellow Springs. May all transcend the realms of suffering and forever escape the dark ford. May nine generations of ancestors ascend to heaven, and six relations receive blessings. May disasters vanish before they arise, and goodness flow without end. We dedicate this for the peace of our household, praying for supreme fortune.

*Huang Qi’s Yellow Register Rite Prayer for Two Deceased Sons*

Your servant has heard that the supreme Dao, embracing all phenomena, stands as the honored nurturer of creation, while the Heavenly Worthy, in vast salvation of all beings, expounds the Way of Emptiness. Its grace extends to the minutest dust, its blessings embrace both the living and the dead. The Perfected Ones reveal the jade-chamber scriptures, releasing those in the long night from the suffering of dense yin. Sincere devotion ascends to move the unseen, and mysterious favor must surely arrive. Yet your servant’s past transgressions have long been manifest, and the divine has sent down its reproof. Within barely a month, two sons have been lost in succession. In the desolation of middle age, I stand alone, a solitary shadow. During the season of ancestral offerings, I have cut off all thoughts of the dark beyond. How then may I aid those wandering souls still bound and detained? Reflecting on their deliverance, I can only rely upon these rites of burning and cultivation. Setting aside the resources for mourning garments, I instead assist this assembly of fragrant lamps. May the cool breeze harmonize with the chime of bells, heard amidst the melodies of the Yellow Springs; may the autumn moon congeal over the altar, illuminating the terraces of the night. Through the merit of this fast, may they together pass the gates of darkness. May their souls be refined in the Vermilion Palace and their spirits born in the Crimson Mansion. May each follow the path of carefree wandering and all ascend to the realm of purity. May they forever serve the true and upright, eternally dwelling in the domain of the Dao. In the human world and the heavens above, may they meet again in good affinity at the end of time; through ten thousand kalpas and a thousand lives, may they reunite with their kin. This luminous vow, the true sages surely perceive. I cannot contain my weeping and reverent prayers.

*Three Hymns by Zhao Gao to Assist the Shangyuan Yellow Register Rite*

The supreme Dao flows with compassion, and the Primordial August One bestows its favor. The Three Palaces and Four Amnesties extend their trust and grant absolution...

The myriad beings shine in glory, rejoicing together in the spring-like grace of the Dao. The imperial altar bestows its vast protection, leaving none in darkness or light unblessed. I, though foolish and unworthy, have been favored by the sacred mandate, early receiving the grace of rank and emolument, ever vigilant against complacency. Yet I fear that within the span of years and the movements of the stars, I may encounter adversity and misfortune, and thus my apprehension runs deep. Taking this opportunity of the Yellow Register Daoist sanctuary, I humbly offer repentance and gratitude, looking up to the exalted sages and beseeching them to look down upon my sincerity. May they secretly bestow blessings and prosperity, silently dispel calamities and faults, augment my years and vitality, and grant well-being to my family. May the living and the departed, the seen and the unseen, together attain radiant protection.

**Middle Prime**
The season shifts as the summer’s heat yields to autumn’s purity. The drum of the *Yize* resounds in the western suburbs, and the fiery clouds gather at the southern pole. This is a time to cease wrongdoing and guard against evil, truly befitting this sacred occasion. Though I am but dust in the mortal realm, I have been graced to partake in the transformation of the Dao. My body serves the Vermilion Register, and my name is inscribed in the Mystic Terrace. Yet my transgressions accumulate easily, and the snares of the world are hard to escape. In movement and stillness, action and retreat, I have not merged with the Great Dao; in the passage of years and the configurations of the stars, I remain entangled in manifold afflictions. Thus, I take this occasion of the Yellow Register’s sacred altar to assist in the offering of incense and devotion. I hope to receive the power of the sages and have my humble sincerity beheld. May the scrolls of sin be unsealed and transgressions absolved, may worldly burdens be lifted and hardships dispelled. May the Nine Mysteries receive this grace, and my entire clan be blessed with honor. I vow to forever uphold the mercy of their protection and devote myself to their worship.

**Lower Prime**
By virtue of past causes, I have received accumulated blessings. Early in life, I assumed official duties, and my family has been undeservedly honored with rank. Yet the responsibilities I bear are weighty and difficult, and my apprehension runs deep. I still fear that the passing years may bring misfortune, and the stars may cast their baleful influence. Should I encounter hardship and obscurity, I would have no recourse for prayer. Now, as the Dark Emperor governs the season and the Lord of Waters presides over the time, the stellar handle points to early winter, and the northern constellations command the frosty air. The year’s light wanes, and my devotion grows ever more earnest. Thus, I dare to approach the altar of the Nine Offerings, reverently gazing upon the exalted sages. Pouring forth my myriad supplications, I pray for their boundless compassion. May my sins and faults be dissolved, and my misfortunes cease. May past grievances and karmic debts be pacified through merit and virtue; may past lives and the present be uplifted through repentance and prayer. May the Nine Mysteries enjoy blessings, and my entire clan be graced with honor. I vow to forever uphold the mercy of their protection and devote myself to their worship.

---

**Feng Juan, Grand Master for Assisting the Prime, Offers Hymns for the Upper Prime Yellow Register Rite**
I prostrate myself, acknowledging that the Great Dao bestows its scriptures, its grace extending to both the living and the departed; the Heavenly Worthy expounds its teachings, its mercy reaching the seen and unseen. It broadly establishes the ninefold ordinances to deliver those in deepest darkness from suffering. With sorrowful sincerity, I dare to knock upon the mystic gate. On the twenty-sixth day of this month, it is the memorial fast for my late mother, the Lady of Longxi Commandery, posthumously honored as the Grand Lady of Longxi Commandery, née Li. I have come to the Jade Bureau’s sacred altar to participate in the Upper Prime’s grand assembly, offering incense and devotion to pray for blessings. I humbly pray that my late mother may refine her spirit in the Vermilion Mansion and dwell in the Mystic Garden. May she awaken to the Dao of tranquility, stillness, and emptiness, and attain the truth of eternal life through kalpas. May she realize the unfettered assembly of the Dao and achieve its wondrous fruit.

**Middle Prime**
I have heard that the luminous ordinances of the Yellow Register and the august canons of the Purple Yang, through the sublime power of the Primordial August One, proclaim grace upon the cinnabar tablets, delivering the submerged in darkness and illuminating the night of the unseen. From ancient times to the present, all who receive its teachings, in life and death, bear its grace. Where there is sincerity, there is response; what is prayed for shall be granted. On the twenty-sixth day of this month, the anniversary of my late mother, the posthumously honored Grand Lady of Longxi Commandery, I take this occasion of the Jade Bureau’s altar and the Middle Prime’s rites to offer devotion, hoping to reach her true spirit. I humbly pray that my late mother, by this blessed affinity, may ascend to the realm of the Dao, wander the azure heavens, and shed her form in the Vermilion Terrace. May she forever dwell in the land of joy and realize the Dao of tranquility and emptiness.

**Lower Prime**
As the Dark Emperor governs the season and the Lord of Waters orders the time, the grand assembly of the Lower Prime arrives, a day of great pardon and prosperity. It is fitting to reverently pray to the exalted sages, who in turn bestow their grace upon the earth below, bringing auspicious blessings to the living and the dead. Now, at the Jade Bureau’s sacred precinct, the jade altar is arrayed for the rites. I humbly present the ritual tokens to assist in the sincerity of the fast. I dare to hope that the host of sages will deign to descend and the myriad perfected ones will shine their protection. May the Nine Mysteries be delivered, transcending the desolate realm of darkness; may the five clans harmonize and forever enjoy the blessings of peace and stability. May misfortunes cease and sins be absolved. I forever pledge my devotion and look up to receive this vast grace.

---

**Zhou Xiang, Gentleman for Court Audiences, Offers Hymns for the Upper Prime Yellow Register Rite**
I have heard that the fasts of the nine ranks are observed, and the festivals of the Three Primes commence. This is the time when all directions pray for blessings, the day when the host of sages proclaim their grace. Now, as the true transformation of the Primordial August One unfolds at the Jade Bureau’s sacred altar, the rites of the Yellow Register are arrayed, and the ordinances of the Mystic Capital are followed. For nine periods, offerings are made; for three days, the fast is observed. With incense and lamps, repentance and purification are jointly offered. I humbly pray that the exalted ones will bestow their protection, that the Great Dao will extend its compassion, that my sincerity will be received, and that vast blessings will be conferred. May the nine generations of ancestors fulfill their wish for ascension, and the six relations be graced with the benevolence of their shelter. May future hardships be dispelled and past enmities resolved. May sins be absolved and illnesses healed. May longevity and emolument be augmented, and misfortunes eradicated. May I ever embody the virtue of renewal and never forget the grace of the Great Dao.
