Thus, we have undertaken its renewal and reconstruction, striving to honor our labors. As the years pass, we deeply fear disturbances may arise. Therefore, we present this jiao offering to pacify and restore the dragon spirits.

May the nation enjoy peace and the people harmony, the times prosperity and customs abundance. May the great mandate be exalted and the mysterious blessings perpetually bestowed. [We dare not say more.]

---

**Jiao Petition for the Hua-Long Pond in the Central Plains**

When the Three Qi were divided, the Five Spirits gave rise to the dragon. It governs the mechanism of creation and transformation, mastering the subtleties of ascent and descent. Its divine power resides in the celestial image of Qian, while its mysterious virtue is nurtured in the palace of Kan.

Long ago, our ancestor, the Illustrious Emperor, inspected the lands of Shu. There, he witnessed its soaring flight, a true manifestation of auspicious omens. Thus, he ordered the excavation of a pond to provide it a fitting abode. Now, the years have passed, and the embankments lie in ruins. Weeds choke the waves, and sand seals the springs. Yet the numinous presence remains undiminished, and its offerings are still conveyed. Each time, it bestows the grace of timely rain, fulfilling the hopes of the parched farmers.

Mindful of this legacy, we are deeply moved. We, of meager virtue, have inherited the mandate and govern a time beset by rebels. As we inspect the lands and tour the customs, we remain encamped in the southern plains. May the dragon display its thunderous might and shake its wind-borne commands. Sweep away the bandits from the northern lands and clear the mists from the Central Plains. May governance be harmonious and just, and boundless blessings perpetually bestowed. [We dare not say more.]

**Prayer for the Emperor’s Birthday by the Crown Prince**

We have heard that the vast heavens cover all without need of reverent prayers, and the azure seas embrace even the tiniest dewdrop. Daring to follow this principle, we now offer our utmost sincerity.

On the day of this month and year, the Emperor’s birthday, his natal hour falls upon *jiaxu*. The secret records of the Primordial Heaven foretold his radiant blessings, and the earth’s profound depths bore auspicious omens, silently aligning with the luminous scriptures. The divination of his years unfolds the glory of ten thousand generations, and the reckoning of his reign reveals the aid of a hundred spirits. Thus, we conduct this grand *jiao* ceremony, reverently awaiting boundless grace. May the blessings of the Three Origins and the myriad sages converge, granting him the longevity of the North Star and the Southern Mountains. With resplendent devotion, we humbly beseech the mysterious favor.

We, your subject [Name], prostrate ourselves in earnest supplication.

---

**Prayer for the Descent of the Crane at Pengnü Abbey by the River Lord, Great King**

We reflect that the Dao’s transformations are boundless, and the perfected immortals manifest in the ethereal and indistinct. Within the subtle and imperceptible, they display the forms of the mysterious and the yellow. Gazing down upon the mortal realm, they deliver all beings. Their deeds are recorded in scriptures and illustrated in sacred texts.

Thus, when Ding Ling returned, he was seen with a crimson crest; when Su Dan descended, his frost-white plumage was revealed. Their tales have become timeless legends, and their auspicious signs were inscribed in the annals of their eras.

Now, we suddenly hear that a numinous crane has alighted upon Cloud Peak—a mountain where the Primordial One wandered and taught, the very place where Peng Zu ascended to heaven. The sacred altar lies secluded, long untouched by offerings of incense, yet the dense forests have indeed brought forth this wondrous response. Truly, this is a supreme omen of our sagely dynasty, not something summoned by a mere regional lord.

We pray for the mountain’s longevity and the crane’s enduring years, to honor the dragon’s chart and the phoenix’s calendar. Gazing afar at the mist-shrouded peaks, we are filled with awe and joy. Hoping to convey our devotion through the rites of this *jiao* ceremony, we humbly present our supplication.

We respectfully dispatch the Purple-Robed Great Virtue, Shangguan Zizhen, Commander of the Army, Wang Chengchen, to offer incense and fire with utmost sincerity, addressing the perfected spirits.

We prostrate ourselves in reverent prayer.

Volume Sixteen of the *Guangcheng Collection*
*Jiao* Prayer for the Enfeoffment of the Two Perfected, Li, at the Heavenly-Bestowed Observance
Composed by Du Guangting, Great Virtue of the Inner Chapel of the Supreme Clarity Palace in the Upper Capital, Purveyor of Imperial Compositions, Granted the Purple Robe

We humbly observe that when former kings examined the charts and received the Mandate, they necessarily bore the profound favor of the Dao to assist in establishing their august foundations. Yet when the seas and mountains faced manifold crises and the people had no refuge, they were then elevated by acclamation and swiftly settled the lands of Min and Bo. Though tribute from the four directions arrived, the mountains and rivers of the central realm remained obstructed. Anxiously seeking governance, they toiled from dawn to dusk, honing spears and halberds, issuing stern commands. They awaited the execution of punitive expeditions to rescue the imperiled—not out of a preference for fine weaponry, but to quell the many calamities. With such deep concern, their distress and labor doubled.

Yet the regional lords of the commanderies and kingdoms have repeatedly presented auspicious omens: creatures of scale, shell, feather, and fur gathering among the forests, bamboo groves, and trees. Some display extraordinary forms, others bear patterns that manifest near and far. Each time, we have modestly declined, repeatedly suppressing their reports.

In the autumn of the second year of Yongping, in the seventh month, an ancient bronze prophecy inscribed in seal script was discovered at Ling Mountain in Xianju. It was the *Record of the Supreme One’s Communication with Heaven*, a text cast by Perfected Zhang. Names, birth dates, and the years of descendants were set forth in layer upon layer of revelation, each detail aligning perfectly. Like the Duke of Zhou divining with millet stalks or Guo Pu casting yarrow, this was truly a gift from Heaven, its divine efficacy proven beyond doubt. Overwhelmed by my own inadequacy, how dare I fail in reverent devotion?

Thus, a new abbey was established, and a propitious name bestowed. Its rituals of image and offering were prepared, and the name of the garrison county was changed. Golden registers were purified in fasting, and jade altars were consecrated in libation. Though my sincerity in offering thanks is manifest, it scarcely repays the bounty of the Supreme Mystery.

Perfected Zhang personally sealed the sacred script, while Perfected Li was the first to guard the immortal mountain. Together, they brought harmony to auspicious omens, illuminating all the kingdoms. It is fitting to confer honors in recognition of their meritorious aid. Invoking the enduring statutes, I humbly submit this petition of inadequacy.

Hereby, Zhang Hongdao is enfeoffed as Perfected of Mirroring Sagacity, and Li Babai as Perfected of Mystic Response. I respectfully dispatch the Venerable Master of Broad Completion, Duke Du Guangting of Cai, Grand Master for Glorious Happiness and Left Grand Master of Remonstrance, to prepare incense and lamps with utmost devotion and perform the libation rites.

May the gates of the Ninefold Purity open, and the cloud-chariot of the Eight Radiant Sceneries descend. Look down upon my luminous sincerity, and bestow your boundless grace.

May the Nine Provinces and Six Directions sweep away all miasmic vapors to become your domain; may earth endure and heaven stretch long, merging chariots and writings into a single transformative influence. I vow to uphold the mysterious teachings and forever cultivate the cinnabar heart.

With utmost reverence, I offer this prayer.

---

**Imperial Edict Conferring Title upon Perfected Zhang**

Your name is inscribed upon the cinnabar registers, for heaven has bestowed upon you immortal talent. In the mortal realm, jade scrolls and pearl-adorned carriages have never drawn your gaze; beyond the world, you dwell among clouds, drink from the dawn, and find serene tranquility. Early on, you received the sacred scriptures and mastered the subtle portents of heaven and earth. You delved into hidden depths, foreseeing the future from the past. Engraving bronze with celestial seals upon the immortal mountain, you bore witness to the Metal Phase in the kingdom of Shu. For over two hundred years, your traces have remained concealed, yet ever renewed are the fifty-eight characters that cycle through, verifying every auspicious sign.

Though my virtue is meager, I reverently receive your numinous grace. Though I have built resplendent halls and sculpted august likenesses, inscribed the names of new cities, and performed the rites of purification and offering, my humble heart remains unfulfilled, unable to repay your boundless favor. Thus, I now invoke the rites of state to specially confer honors and exaltation.

Now conferring upon you the title of **Perfected Master of Illuminating Sagacity**, I reverently dispatch Du [Mou] to inaugurate the frost-altar rites and solemnly proclaim this edict.

Phoenix carriages and crane bridles shall attend your journey in the footsteps of Wen Shi; jade chambers and vermilion curtains shall array you among the ranks of Tai Yuan. May the Perfected Master continue to bestow subtle aid, ever lending your numinous radiance, that the Nine Domains be unified under one rule and the Great Enterprise endure in eternal prosperity. Through diligent toil from dawn to dusk, may the people live in peace.

With utmost reverence, the edict.

**Edict Conferring the Title of Perfected Master Li**

Your immortal plum branch, fragrant and golden, parts the clouds with its lineage. From the Dark Mound you set your resolve, though your talent was never bound by fleeting time; your Dao-bone and true wind originally ranked among the ranks of long life. Shaking your robes beyond the world, you soared aloft amid the clouds. Weary of the toil of swift passage like a foal’s window or lightning’s flight, you found the joy of riding clouds upon Ao Ridge. Dwelling and wandering in the kingdom of Shu, you appeared and vanished amid the dusty world. Thrice you concealed yourself on Spirit Peak, living over eight hundred years. Your elixir transformed stone, still abiding on Changli Mountain; your entire household ascended to heaven, thus marking the immortal’s dwelling. Here, upon the old site, the numinous script was indeed discovered—long sealed in the jade ruins, now revealed to accord with the Metal Phase. Reflecting upon my deficient virtue, I humbly bear this extraordinary grace. Though I have repaired and adorned your sacred foundations, reverently arrayed your august likeness, led the assembly in solemn rites of thanksgiving, and commanded the feather-robed to perform the burning offerings, my humble heart remains unfulfilled, unable to repay your profound power. Now, having examined the proper rites, I offer this fine title. May you, clad in starry pendants and rosy robes, swiftly ascend to your true rank; and may dew-sealed vermilion script express my earnest devotion. Reflecting upon my modest bearing, I am deeply abashed.

Now conferring upon you the title of **Perfected Master of Mystic Response**, I reverently dispatch Du Guangting to establish the offering altar and solemnly proclaim this edict. May your mystic shade flow forth to eternally bless the imperial foundation. Hearing the distant thoughts of the Hall of Audience, I await the gaze of the exalted Perfected.

With utmost reverence, the edict.

**Prayer of the Grand Marshal of Hanzhou at the Immortal’s Abode Altar**

Your servant has heard that the supreme Dao, non-action itself, embraces the myriad heavens to accomplish transformation; its dark efficacy, though active, governs the Four Symbols to mold and refine. Its encompassing vastness has never faltered from ancient times to the present. Thus the Three Spirits are ordered, the Five Wefts follow their course, auspicious blessings extend to hidden companions, and great blessings overflow through states and kingdoms. Heaven and humanity depend upon it, receiving its profound moisture in distant reaches.

Your servant, long moved by your numinous compassion, has encountered this flourishing fortune. Repeatedly receiving extraordinary favors, I have been honored with the dignity of the bamboo tally; frequently bathed in profound grace, I have been entrusted with weighty and difficult duties. Yet, reflecting upon my emptiness and meagerness, I have achieved no meritorious deeds. Mindful of my duty to share the sovereign’s burdens, I tremble with awe. Though I devote my heart and strength, vowing to repay the private bonds of ruler and father, I fear that blessings overreaching may invite calamity, or that I may tread the path of obscurity and delusion.

I privately fear that in commanding troops and governing borders, ruling the people entails the burdens of litigation, and fulfilling office involves the breadth of taxes and corvée. Encouragement and deterrence require the use of rewards and punishments; sending off and receiving involve customary feasts and rewards. There are concerns over accidental injuries and misjudgments in severity or leniency. Thus, offenses accumulate, yet I have never performed rites of repentance and prayer. Perhaps past debts and former grievances remain unresolved; or celestial patterns and fate’s course still align with calamitous times. From early summer to autumn’s moon, I have long suffered minor ailments, yet to be cured.

Without relying on the grace of the supreme Dao, who could summon the protection of the true numina? Now, as the jade altar is arrayed and the purple-sealed edict descends, may the exalted immortals pause their chariots in response, and the myriad sages manifest to bestow blessings. Daring to seize this propitious gathering, I humbly prepare fragrant offerings, laying bare my sincere devotion and reverently praying for your mystic shade. I prostrate myself, beseeching your guardianship and the granting of good fortune. May my offenses and faults be swept away, grievances resolved, calamities transcended, and years and blessings increased. May illness and misfortune vanish, and auspicious signs gather. May the altar masters and ritualists diligently serve the sages with devotion; beneath the azure canopy and vermilion wheels, I dare not neglect the arrival of spring’s procession.

I cannot express the fullness of my devotion in returning to life and baring my heart.

With utmost reverence, the prayer.

**Prayer for the Natal Destiny of Former Military Commissioner of Jiazhou, Sikong Wang Zongjie**

---

I humbly acknowledge that the two qi govern the movements of the cosmos, and the Five Agents bring forth transformation. All who receive form and destiny owe their existence to the Supreme Mystery. Yet I, with my meager endowments, have presumptuously enjoyed the grace of nurturing cultivation. By good fortune, I have encountered an era of prosperity and repeatedly been honored with favor. Within, I have served in the inner chambers of the court; without, I have been entrusted with the stewardship of rivers and mountains. I have overseen the military, governing the common people. Ashamed of my lack of talent for governance, I have ever feared the warning against excess. Indeed, I have encountered adversity and thus fallen into peril. Yet through the profound mercy of the sagely and enlightened, I have been restored to the ranks of the gentry. Rising early and retiring late, I am ever mindful of the imperial grace and kindness. My heart is filled with devotion, yet my meager service has not repaid the sovereign and father.

For years now, misfortunes have lingered unceasingly. Since mid-autumn, illness has struck repeatedly. Though I have sought medical treatment, recovery has eluded me. I note that Saturn has resided in the palace of my life and destiny for several years; Mars has lingered in the position of fields and dwellings, still in the northern quadrant. The Year Star has become an omen of the Six Harms, and my minor fate coincides with the year’s destruction. Though the advent of Jupiter at winter’s onset brings fortune, I am presently afflicted by the misfortunes of my current fate. Beset by this inauspicious decline, my anxiety deepens.

Moreover, I fear that the affairs of governance may be fraught with grave difficulties. In administering punishments, I may lack compassion; in overseeing provisions, I may err in preparation. Long-standing karmic debts remain unexpiated, and my prayers of repentance have been incomplete. I also fear that past transgressions may have been recorded in the hidden registers, or that the dragon spirits of my residence may have been offended by solitude. Perhaps the tombs of my homeland have suffered damage, bringing calamity upon me and causing this peril. With remorse, I reflect upon my faults and turn earnestly to prayer.

Daring to seize this day of my natal destiny, I reverently prepare offerings of incense and lamps. Gazing toward the mysterious heavens, I plead for life, pouring forth my sincere devotion in hope of grace. I prostrate myself before the true spirits of Heaven and Earth, the lords of yin and yang. May they bestow their vast protection and heed my deepest sincerity. May my sins and faults be swept away, my calamities dispelled. May grievances be resolved, and the flow of misfortune dissolved. May my ancestors find peace in the netherworld, and my descendants enjoy tranquility in this sagely age. May the three barriers and pores of my body know no obstruction, and the six viscera and their mechanisms find balance and harmony. Grant me recovery and bless me with good fortune. Extend my years in this autumn of near-exhaustion, and preserve my life in this day of rebirth. With heart laid bare and tears shed, I offer my most earnest prayers. I vow to devote myself to reverent service, repaying the protection of the exalted spirits.

With utmost reverence, the prayer.

**Prayer for the Shangyuan Offering by Former Prefect of Hanzhou, Lord Zongkui**

I have heard that the Dao shapes Heaven and Earth, molding yin and yang. The Three Origins serve as the seasons of transformation, and the Five Peaks govern the records of life. Their authority culminates in the Perfect Truth, enabling blessings to extend to the state and grace to embrace both the seen and unseen. The Vermilion Registers of Nanchang expand the path of virtue, while the Black Scripts of the Northern Bureau reveal the principles of correction. Thus are warnings and encouragements issued, and the protection of all beings extended. Having received the true teachings, I have ever adhered to their luminous instructions, striving with diligence to fulfill the mysterious compassion.

I reflect upon the depth of the state’s grace and the insufficiency of my efforts to serve the sovereign. My achievements remain unrecorded in the tripods, yet my honors surpass those of all ministers. Abroad, I have borne the banner and tassel, commanding the military; at home, I have received fresh favors and ascended to lofty ranks. The green gates of the inner court mark my exalted position, and the yellow pivots of power signify my heavy responsibilities. With humility, I am filled with awe, yet I find no means to repay my lord.

Thus, I devoutly perform these rites of incense and prayer, hoping to repay the kindness of sovereign and kin. Now, as the Celestial Officials govern the seasons and the Great White One presides over the directions, the Lesser Yin bestows its nurturing warmth, and the Great Amnesty issues decrees of creation. With utmost sincerity, I hold fast to the fragrant flames and reverently commence this offering. Gazing toward the celestial signs, I concentrate my heart, awaiting the response of auspicious omens.

Above all, I pray that the precious chart may endure, and the sagely lifespan be prolonged. May all within and without enjoy peace, and the realm know tranquility. May the Eight Extremities and Nine Lands be united under one sovereign; may the years be bountiful, the qi harmonious, and the governance ever free from strife. May the netherworld be bright and serene, and all living things flourish. May the land and all beneath Heaven ascend to the realm of longevity.

I, your subject, beseech that calamities be swept away, karmic debts resolved. May sins and faults be erased, and blessings gathered. May both public and private affairs prosper, and my family remain ever at peace. I vow to devote my heart to loyalty and filial piety, aiding the flourishing of this enlightened age.

**Prayer for the Illness and Misfortune of the Lady of Zhao State**

I have heard that the heavenly truth pities all beings, and the great Dao cherishes life. Ever extending its rescuing compassion, it fulfills the wish for safety. Behold the supreme transformation, nurturing all living things. The two qi, in their misty union, shape form; the Three Origins, in their radiance, determine destiny. Fortune and misfortune, sin and blessing, are all ordained by the celestial authorities.

I, however, am burdened by a destiny and fate both in decline, with my natal tone residing in the tomb. Though I have encountered the auspiciousness of the House Spirit, I am also beset by the inauspiciousness of clashes and destruction. My wandering year coincides with the Celestial Talisman, and my natal destiny encounters the Five Ghosts. Within my life palace, hidden malevolent stars entangle me. Saturn has lingered in my dull and stagnant fate, while on the position of punishment and misfortune, Mars has repeatedly converged. Thus, calamity has manifested as illness, and recovery has not come, deepening my anxiety.

I fear that sins from past lives and this existence remain unresolved, and karmic debts of life and wealth unpaid. Without the grand altar of this great offering, my earnest prayers of repentance cannot be fully expressed. Therefore, I set aside my garments and ornaments, preparing these fragrant offerings. Solemnly arranging the altar, I reverently present my prayers.

I prostrate myself before the myriad heavens, entreating their compassion and protection, and the multitude of sages, beseeching their mercy. May they extend their benevolence of rebirth and fulfill the virtue of cherishing life. May the Three Officials and Five Emperors, the hidden malevolent stars and Seven Origins, the Southern Dipper and Northern Star, the celestial authorities and constellations, the sacred peaks and rivers, the luminous spirits of the earthly courts, and the deities of my natal palace, wandering year, and the inner and outer Eight Trigrams—may all the responsive spirits of the Three Realms, within the registers of the celestial bureaus and the records of destiny, pardon my grievances, sins, and transgressions, and the calamities and misfortunes ordained by fate. Grant me the continuation of my blessings and years, and the extension of my lifespan.

---

May it sweep away misfortune and decline, and dispel illness and suffering.
May the hundred meridians flow freely, and the six viscera find peace and harmony.
May I once more behold the light of heaven and again tread the affairs of men.
With heart laid bare and resolve strengthened, I shall forever repay the grace of salvation and aid;
Contemplating goodness and delving into the mysteries, I aspire to fully receive the blessings of the true spirits.

Unable to contain the earnestness of my pleading, I humbly beseech for life and destiny, my devotion and supplication most fervent.

Respectfully submitted.

*Petition for the Grand Offering on the Day of the Holy Descent of the Lady of Hongnong Commandery at the Residence of Wang Zongjie*

I, your humble servant, have heard that the Primordial Daoist Ancestor, the Most High Lord Lao, abides in the Three Realms, ever mindful of all under heaven, and in his compassion for salvation, descends in true form.
He bestows the five-colored radiance of the Great Yang and ascends with the nine dragons of the rising sun.
His dream took shape by the Luo River, and his birth was beneath the immortal plum.
Lotus blossoms opened upon the earth as he first received the jade steps;
A well sprang forth in the empty courtyard, its waters cleansing his jade-like form.
His august countenance revealed his singular bearing, and his sagely decrees expounded the subtle teachings.
The myriad heavens took him as their foundation, and successive generations regarded him as their master.
He marked the propitious day with a festival, bestowing extraordinary blessings upon all beings.
It is fitting to honor this grand assembly and manifest our utmost sincerity.

I, your servant, early awakened to the true vehicle and have long studied the sacred registers.
The wondrous scriptures of life extension, the texts of the Purple Yang and Cinnabar Palace;
The divine charts of transformation, the records of the Crimson Towers and Vermilion Palaces.
I align body and mind within the Nine Chambers, and regulate spirit and qi at the Three Passes.
I cleanse transgressions and dispel evil, benefiting both the hidden and the manifest.
Ever diligent in my devotion, I dare not cease the offerings of incense and lamps.

Now, on this occasion of great amnesty, I reverently prepare the rites for the offering to the true spirits.
Thus, I send forth my sincerity to the crane pavilions and fix my gaze upon the dragon chariots.
With heartfelt devotion, I present my words, and upon the jade altar, I complete the rites.
From the celestial palaces to the earthly courts, from the solar domains to the stellar paths,
The bureaus of the Three Officials and Five Emperors, the northern and southern celestial offices,
Below, encompassing the rivers and mountains, and all around, pervading the hidden spirits—
I exhaust my bright sincerity, hoping for their luminous regard.

Above, I pray that the imperial foundation may endure forever, and the sagely lifespan extend far and long.
May the Dao flourish in harmony, and the sacred teachings spread abroad.
In the nine regions and four frontiers, may the winds of virtue and power be ever revered;
May all beings and myriad creatures together enjoy the fortune of peace and prosperity.
May my ninefold ancestors and sevenfold forebears, the departed spirits of old,
Ascend to the cinnabar mounds and be born in the azure heavens.
May disasters be averted before they arise, and goodness descend without limit.
May my years be increased, and my sins and transgressions all absolved.
I vow to remain steadfast in devotion, fully receiving your vast compassion.

Unable to contain the utmost of my submission to destiny.

*Birthday Petition of the Prefect of Yangzhou*

I prostrate myself, for the Three Heavens spread their transforming influence, and the Orthodox Unity bestows its teachings.
Their wondrous works shine forth, broadly aiding all beings,
Desiring that the light of heaven illuminate the hidden gates below, stilling the sorrows of the unseen;
That the humblest pleas ascend to the radiant sun above, fulfilling the wish for unimpeded communication.
Thus, they unfolded the Twenty-Four Registers, appointed the Twelve Hundred Officials,
To govern humanity and oversee the true records.
They dispatch spirit riders as couriers and waft fragrant stalks as messenger dragons.
Through accumulated thought, resonance may be expected; through salvation and protection, sincerity and clarity will surely reach them.
From ancient times to the present, their veneration has been profound, and their beneficence manifest.

Your servant has long admired the Orthodox and True, ever receiving the shade of their protection.
Though I have held the altar seal and ministerial tally, I have yet to repay my debt to the state;
Purifying myself and clarifying my mind, I have ever been earnest in my desire for self-cultivation.
Now, I reverently receive the imperial decree and temporarily govern the distant frontier.
On the occasion of my birthday, I humbly seek divine favor,
Reverently presenting the offering rites and meticulously preparing this petition.

I beseech the Great Dao to extend its compassion, and the Heavenly Master to grant his regard and protection.
May the martial officials and generals descend to cover and shield me.
May my garrison duties be accomplished, and the beacons of war fall silent.
May the distant lands turn anew, all swaddled infants carried to embrace benevolence;
May the fierce and unruly reform their hearts, all climbing the mountains to turn toward the Dao.
I await the cleansing of the world, that lasting harmony may prevail.

May your servant’s official emoluments and lifespan be increased, and misfortunes and calamities cease.
May the fortunes of the Dao be secure and prosperous, and the generals and officials harmonious.
May the hidden and the manifest alike receive the mysterious blessings.

Unable to contain the utmost of my submission and fervent supplication.

Respectfully offered.

**Eastern Court Minister of Education’s First Month Jiazi Offering**

We humbly acknowledge that the Great Dao sheds its radiance, and the Mysterious Origin bestows its transformation. Qi divides into the Five Wefts, where the Five Emperors hold the power of cyclical change; the seasons unfold through the Three Origins, where the Three Officials govern the records of life and death. Thus, the hundred spirits receive their offices, and all things know their place. Cold and heat alternate, completing the year’s work and revealing retribution; the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches align, ordering human affairs and determining fortune and misfortune. From ancient times to the present, this has been reverently observed, and the numinous never fails to respond.

Your servant, undeservingly sheltered by the Dao’s shade, has been granted the fortune to assist in this flourishing age. Yet blessings may turn to calamity, and I ever heed the warning of holding too full a measure; my talents are slight, but my duty is weighty, and I can only offer my utmost sincerity in serving the state. Now, as the season reaches the Upper Prime and the cycle renews the Six Jia, we examine the records at the head of the Celestial Office, where the first Jiazi of the new reckoning is observed. On this auspicious day, I reverently conduct the great offering.

Dare I hope the Mysterious Sage will deign to regard my earnest devotion?

Your servant reflects that, though distant from the court and my parents’ chambers, I remain bound by the rites of filial piety. Now, as I prepare to attend them, I am still hindered by mountains and rivers. Moreover, the winding paths of Long Gorge and the treacherous depths of the Yangtze’s waves weigh upon me. Only by relying on divine power may I hope to safely traverse these perilous roads.

We implore the lofty Five Emperors, the great Three Officials, and the numinous spirits of the sixty Jiazi to turn their responsive might toward this offering and bestow their manifest blessings. May my light vessel cross smoothly, covering ten thousand li without peril. Spare me the lament of climbing hills in sorrow, and swiftly grant me the joy of serving my parents in their old age. May my earnest prayers be fulfilled, and may I never fail in gratitude for this luminous grace.

I vow to uphold my reverent devotion, forever repaying the protection of the true spirits. Unable to contain the utmost of my submission and fervent supplication, I offer this prayer with all my heart.

Respectfully presented.

---

**Offering Prayer of Marshal Zhao, Grand Commandant of Yangping**

We humbly acknowledge that the Perfect Dao scatters its light, and the immortal courts array their ranks. Above, they float among the celestial bodies; below, they bind themselves to renowned mountains. They encompass the cavern-palaces in profound majesty, embracing clouds and mist in their singular splendor. They secretly safeguard the state and broadly shelter all living beings, governing the destinies of humans and heavens, presiding over the registers of life. They dispel disasters and bestow blessings, responding unfailingly to all who call.

Your servant, having received the favor of sagely rule, has been undeservingly honored with rank and emolument. Commanding the military, I am ashamed to lack the achievements of Han Xin or Bai Qi; holding the tally of authority, I am humbled by my failure to match the governance of Gong Sui or Huang Ba. Ever wary of excess, I have brought upon myself misfortune and decline. Thus, I have wholeheartedly turned to the Mysterious Teachings, transmitting and upholding its scriptures and registers, revering its true spirits.

May the fortunes of the state be prolonged and vast, and my lifespan firm and enduring. May the myriad regions be united, and the four seas harmonized as one.

Your servant, having shed the perils of calamity, prays for the absolution of his transgressions. May my six relations receive blessings, and my nine generations ascend to heaven. May my official emoluments and lifespan increase, and my merits and renown be established.

I vow to uphold loyalty and filial piety, forever serving the radiant and enlightened. May my diligent devotion meet the favor of the perfected immortals.

Reverently conducting this offering, I humbly present my sincere plea. Unable to contain the utmost of my submission and fervent supplication.

Respectfully presented.

---

*End of Scroll Sixteen of the Guangcheng Collection*
*Scroll Seventeen of the Guangcheng Collection*

**Prayer for the Revival of the Withered Cypress at Crane Cry Mountain, Composed by Du Guangting, Grand Virtue of Literary Composition by Imperial Commission, Purple-Robed Bestower, of the Supreme Clarity Palace in the Upper Capital**

Of that immortal mountain,
it establishes this southern land.
Mighty, it cradles the deep earth;
elegant, it upholds the vaulted heavens.
Governing the plains and rivers of Luo and Mian,
commanding the scenic grandeur of Min and Emei.
Its peaks bear the sun aloft,
its grottoes shelter the perfected.
Pines and cypresses, lush and towering, stretch into the void;
for a thousand years, its numinous majesty remains solemn and reverent.
Then came the wondrous portent,
manifest in this blessed sanctuary.
The transformative power of the supreme Yang bestowed its grace,
altering the withered cypress, its decayed form.
Tender branches flourish afresh,
scattering fragrant auspicious dew;
dense leaves renew their glory,
stirred by the clear breeze into swaying verdancy.
The hidden praises of immortals and transcendents,
the blessings invoked for the state and the people.
May this profound felicity endure,
and these auspicious boons be everlasting.
Thus, with utmost reverence, we conduct this offering and prayer,
looking up to answer the perfected spirits.
Our hearts concentrate within the Hall of Audience,
our aspirations soar beyond the cloud-capped peaks.
We pray that the Hua and Yi be illuminated in peace,
that seas and mountains rest in tranquility.
May crops and grains flourish in abundance,
and baleful vapors be dispelled and settled.
May we forever uphold our devotion,
to repay the profound favor of the Dao.

With bowed head, we present this respectful prayer.

---

**Prayer for Protection by Minister Li Zhongshun, Minister of Works**

Your servant has heard:
the Dao operates without limit,
the divine power is unfathomable.
Responding to the moment and the thought,
where there is sincerity, there is communion.
The Orthodox Unity transmitted its scriptures,
bestowing treasured texts to succor all beings;
the Alliance of Might established its teachings,
setting forth the rites of offerings to aid the people.
From the ancients to this day,
its grace extends to the manifest and the hidden,
its blessings pervade heaven and humanity.
Your servant has long received the profound compassion of the Dao,
and has been blessed to live in this sagely age.
The celestial favor flows boundlessly,
the human rank is most generous.
Ashamed of my lack of talent for governance,
I deeply fear the excess of such honor and toil.
Moreover, I oversee the military and the guard,
commanding the fish tally in my post.
In rewards and punishments, I may err in fairness;
in laws and decrees, I may misjudge severity or leniency.
The people harbor grievances,
the common folk bear wounds and sighs.
Should any such fault arise,
it would surely invite divine reproach.
I also fear that the five phases and three destinies
may encounter calamitous obscuration.
Dark stars and bright constellations
may align in ominous conjunction.
Or in traversing water and land,
I may offend the dragon spirits.
Or in constructing earth and timber,
I may violate taboos.
Or there may be old enmities and past debts,
or unintended killings and injuries,
each accumulating into transgressions.
Coupled with inauspicious alignments,
these may bring forth illness and affliction,
deepening my trepidation and concern.
Yet I recall that the Great Dao cherishes life,
and the Supreme Perfected established its teachings.
It has set forth the rites of prayer and exorcism,
opened the gates of repentance and gratitude.
Thus, I dare to prepare the altar with reverence,
and meticulously conduct this offering and prayer.
I bow to heaven and repent my faults,
pouring out my earnest pleas for grace.
I implore the Three Realms’ exalted ones,
the Great Saints of the myriad heavens,
to descend with compassionate bestowal,
and look upon this humble dust with mercy.
Command the celestial and terrestrial bureaus,
pervade the yin and yang realms.
Dissolve and dispel calamities and misfortunes,
absolve and pardon transgressions and faults.
Sever the bonds of misfortune and decline,
reconcile and pacify karmic debts.
Eradicate illness and suffering,
calm and secure the hun and po souls.
Harmonize the six qi,
and free the flow of the hundred meridians.
Transform my brief and fleeting fate,
grant me the gift of prolonged years.
May the ten thousand sins and thousand disasters
all be transcended and delivered.
I vow to uphold my devotion with diligence,
looking up to serve the perfected spirits.
Your servant, unable to contain his gratitude for absolution and his fervent pleas for grace,
presents this prayer with utmost sincerity.

Respectfully presented.

---

**Prayer for Offering by the Lady of the Prefecture, Wife of the Minister of Works**

I have heard:
the Great Dao established its precepts,
the Mysterious Perfected set forth its teachings.
The Orthodox Unity possesses rites for beseeching grace,
the River Chart contains texts for repenting faults.
When we reverently invoke the exalted spirits,
they surely grant their luminous scrutiny.
I, [Lady] so-and-so, have long been favored by numinous blessings,
and born into this mortal realm.
Grateful for the shelter of such grace,
I have always been filled with caution and awe.
Recently, I have been afflicted by illness,
and have not yet recovered.
I fear that in my conduct and bearing,
in my thoughts and intentions,
there may have been errors and transgressions,
or offenses and faults.
Or perhaps I have incurred karmic entanglements,
bringing misfortune upon myself.
Or perhaps dark stars and bright constellations
have cast their influence upon me.
Thus, this calamity has bound me,
and has not yet been dispelled.
Day and night, I am filled with anxiety,
daring not rest in peace.
Moreover, within the palace of my body,
the movement of Saturn’s course
has brought my fate to a perilous juncture.
With utmost sincerity, I make this plea,
daring to follow the luminous precepts
and reverently conduct this grand offering.
I implore the Three Treasures and Supreme Saints,
the exalted deities of the Nine Luminaries,
to bestow boundless compassion
and descend their protective power.
Grant me the dissolution of calamities and misfortunes,
the reconciliation of enmities and grudges.
Prolong my years,
increase my blessings and emoluments.
May the hundred illnesses be healed,
the six qi harmonized.
Wash away misfortune and decline,
erase transgressions and faults.
May I forever uphold my devotion,
to repay the profound grace of the Dao.
Unable to contain my gratitude for absolution and my fervent pleas to the perfected,
I present this prayer with utmost sincerity.

Respectfully presented.

---

**Prayer for the Celestial Net by Duke Ji of the Ministry of Works**

Your servant has heard:
the endowment of emoluments and physical form
derives from the transformative power of the Dao.
The prolongation of life and preservation of destiny
depend upon the divine efficacy.
Yet there are the rise and fall of the three destinies,
the alternation of the five phases.
The movement of stars through their courses,
the auspicious and inauspicious omens of hexagrams.
Should one encounter a period of inauspicious alignment,
the purpose of expiatory rites is surely revealed.
Thus, the Mysterious Perfected pities the world,
and the Great Dao cherishes life.
It has established laws to aid humanity,
responding wherever there is sincerity.
The precious texts of the Three Heavens and Orthodox Unity
proclaim the rites for invoking blessings;
the Grand Mysterious River Chart’s offering rituals
initiate the purpose of averting calamities.
From ancient times to the present, they have been revered,
and their protective succor has been abundant.
Your servant has long been favored by numinous grace,
and has personally lived in this illustrious age.
The honors and favors bestowed are extraordinary,
my rank and status surpass the norm.
Reflecting upon myself, I am ever mindful
of the warning against excess;
pledging my heart and strength, I constantly
fear the reckoning of blessings and faults.
Now, the great fortune still resides in the region of Xu,
and the lesser fortune remains in the position of Hai.
Within this year,
both coincide with the Celestial Net.
I fear that every thought and intention
may incur transgressions and faults.
From past lives and former existences,
I may bear hidden flaws.
Though I have diligently cultivated myself,
how can I be free from errors?
Moreover, dark stars move through the Chen division,
and Mars resides in the palace of my body.
Furthermore, my talents are meager for such great favor,
my merits slight for such weighty rank.
I fear that calamities and obstacles may arise,
deepening my trepidation and concern.
Thus, I dare to follow the mysterious scriptures,
reverently and earnestly prepare my sincere plea,
meticulously conduct this offering rite,
and present this prayer with bowed head.

Grateful for past transgressions before the Nine Heavens,
I pray for the grace of the host of sages.
May the true numina deign to witness and reflect,
bestowing abundant blessings in torrential flow.
May the celestial and terrestrial bureaus be commanded,
the yang officials and yin courts be charged.
Pardon the faults of the past,
cleanse the baleful influences yet to come.
Dispel the disasters of lingering stars,
release the snares of the Celestial Net.
Abundantly extend my allotted blessings and emoluments,
increase my years and lifespan.
May my sincere devotion of loyalty and filial piety
forever aid the radiant transformation of sagely governance.
I vow to diligently hone and refine myself,
to fully respond to the mysterious compassion above.
I can do no more than prostrate myself in utmost reverence.

---

Field Chongqian and Lu Zhao, having received the *Lu* Text of the Six Jia,
prostrate ourselves and declare:
As the supreme transformation is about to unfold,
the mysterious scriptures first manifest.
Five thousand characters convey the teaching,
the Six Jia unfold the chart.
First transmitted in the court of Yu Shun,
passed down from the age of the Ji Zhou.
Cultivated within, it congeals the true and returns to the One,
riding the sun and moon to tread the misty heavens;
practiced without, it protects the state and pacifies the people,
bringing well-being to all beings and abundance to the myriad realms.
As the root of the Dharma,
it has been revered through the ages.
We, your servants, have been favored by the mysterious talismans,
and moreover, have encountered the imperial destiny.
The true wind spreads widely,
the wondrous decree is proclaimed afar.
We wish to follow and cultivate it,
eternally pledging to uphold it.
Fitting the auspicious occasion,
we reverently reveal our bright sincerity.
May the primal sages and merged compassion,
the host of perfected ones, cast their discerning light.
Fulfill our earnest wishes,
bestow your majestic radiance.
Let our devotion and resonance be felt,
our merit and practice come to fruition.
Open the deliverance of the Nine Mysteries,
dissolve the accumulation of past transgressions.
May blessings and goodness swiftly arrive,
lifespan and years be increased.
Aid the people and assist the state,
magnify the Dao and proclaim the scriptures.
Forever propagate the wind of purity and stillness,
perfect the Dao of emptiness and tranquility.
I can do no more than prostrate myself in utmost reverence.

---

Fan Yanxu and others, having received the *Lu* Text of the Orthodox Unity,
respectfully submit this plea.

Humbly we acknowledge that the Southern Palace of Orthodox Unity and the Jade Hall of Purple Yang
guard the true registers of radiant yang and seal the numinous charts of soaring transformation.
Below, they may quell malevolent spirits and proclaim the harmony of qi and seasons;
above, they may pacify the realm and assemble the divine immortals.
To protect the state and secure the people has been their constant mandate through the ages.
We, having encountered this sagely era, are bathed in the wind of the Dao.
Early we cast off the clamor of the world, together dwelling in feathered robes.
We aspire to receive and partake, striving diligently in our burning and cultivation.
May the host of sages, in their vast compassion, grant that we harmonize with the ancestral teachings.
Clad in stellar robes and treading the Dipper, may we follow the flying steps of the Nine Heavens;
assisting the world and establishing merit, may we fulfill the efficacy of the great Dao in its timely transformation.
With incense at the hearth and hands pressed in reverence, we prostrate ourselves and pray to the perfected,
eagerly awaiting the mysterious grace, unable to contain our fervent devotion.

Respectfully submitted by Wang Dang for the offering of the jiao and presentation of this plea.

We have heard that the treasured canon of the River Chart descends its jiao rites to aid the people,
and the luminous statutes of Orthodox Unity manifest their textual proclamations to assist transformation.
Both propagate the essentials of the Dao and widely bless living beings.
We, having been entrusted with the mysterious gate and presuming to partake in the secret registers,
find our burning and cultivation often lacking, our transgressions and faults swiftly manifest.
Our duties lie in public service, yet our actions are frequently marred by regret.
At times, in adjudicating lawsuits, rewards and punishments err in their weight;
in instructing and comforting disciples, encouragement and admonition fall short of their commands.
Searching our hearts and examining ourselves, our anxiety grows day and night.
Without relying on the mysterious power, there is no path to repentance and absolution.

Moreover, at the close of the fifth month, earth and fire are poised to enter the palace of the body.
In this distress, we yearn for expiation and deliverance.
Now, with utmost sincerity and offerings of faith,
we beseech the presentation of this plea.
May the Most High and the host of venerables, lords of the Three Heavens’ transformation,
bestow the great mercy of their grace and descend boundless favor.
Command the celestial officials, soldiers, and guards to fulfill their duties in protection.
Grant that our faults and transgressions be swept away, our karmic debts be pacified.
May the Nine Luminaries reverse the calamities of their visitation,
may the Three Destinies cease the misfortunes of their clashes,
that we may attain purity and auspiciousness, ever enjoying smooth passage.
We vow to uphold the sincerity of our hearth and incense,
to repay above the protection of the august spirits.
We cannot express the fullness of our devotion.

**Petition of Diao Zizong, Exhortation to the Grand Marshal, Presented at the Sacred Pool to the Perfected Master Zhu of the Grotto**

We have heard that the wondrous Dao of creation and transformation, in its vast teaching, saves all beings; its mysterious power, ungoverned by self, spreads the breeze of mercy to all things. Ever responsive without hindrance, it delivers and protects without omission. Thus, the azure tablets and cinnabar scriptures continue to record the ranks of those who ascend to Perfection; even the nightly gates of the hidden bureaus are encompassed by the benevolence of refinement and transformation. Like fire passed from torch to torch, its radiance has illumined all ages.

This humble one, born in an era of propitious destiny, has had his name inscribed in the register of the True Vehicle. With each devout offering of incense and prayer, he has secretly yearned for the power of the Dao, hoping to invoke boundless fortune and, above all, repay the grace of his sovereign. He aspires that the Perfected One may ever inspire his cinnabar heart, and that his thoughts may soon join the study of the mysterious registers. His longing is earnest and unceasing; how may he scale the heights of his reverence?

We prostrate ourselves before the Transcendent Lord, whose Dao is unfettered, whose hidden flight outlives the distant crane. Pointing to the Three Mountains, he soars aloft—none can trace his cloud-borne path; though he returns but briefly after countless years, one can only imagine his sorrow for the dust-bound world. This humble one, shamed by the faintest echoes of Lu Ao’s footsteps, gazes after the distant traces of the Perfected Master as if beholding the tracks of Ruoshi. With a heart poured out in sincerity, he purifies himself, kindles incense, and bows in worship.

We await the turning of the Perfected One’s gaze, that he may deign to bathe us in the dark waves of the Dao. May we, in the midst of our cultivation and study, glimpse even slightly the subtleties of the profound. By disciplining ourselves with utmost sincerity, we shall forever requite the kindness of sovereign and father; by preserving purity and wholeness of truth, we vow to follow in the footsteps of the divine immortals. We cannot express the fullness of our devotion.

Memorial for the Black Talisman Rite by the Grand Tutor and Chancellor

We have heard that the Supreme Dao has bequeathed its precepts, and the Orthodox Unity tradition has established rites of prayer and supplication; the *Hetu* has set forth its teachings, and the Great Mystery has opened the gates of repentance and gratitude. Such is the means to succor and protect human relations and to magnify the power of the Dao. Its grace and blessings have spread far and wide, revered through the ages as the ultimate source.

This humble servant, favored by the fortune of the times, has been entrusted with weighty responsibilities. Though I have striven with utmost sincerity to serve the state, my contributions remain but a drop in the ocean. Fearing that excess fortune may invite calamity, I have suffered affliction and illness. Now, as the Black Talisman takes flight and transforms, entering the Five Agents into the Central Palace, and as my natal destiny and resonant tones align, the severity of this misfortune has grown. Thus, I dare to turn my mind to the profoundest mysteries, bowing my head before the purified altar. With reverence, I prepare incense and lamps, offering solemn prayers and invocations.

May the Primordial One deign to look upon us, and may the Five Emperors extend their compassion. Let them command the noble deities of the Nine Palaces and the officials of the Three Bureaus to dissolve and dispel ill fortune, to harmonize and release enmities and grudges. May they cleanse away transgressions and stains, and augment my allotted span of prosperity. Let all ailments be soothed and long-standing illnesses healed. I vow to pour forth a heart of loyalty and filial piety, hoping to invoke the sagely and enlightened blessings. Forever shall I uphold the wondrous Dao, aspiring to reflect the boundless grace of the Mysterious. I cannot express the fullness of my devotion.

The Magistrate of Yangzhou, Lord Zongkui, and the Lady of Chen State, née [X]氏, prostrate themselves to present this memorial with the Nine Luminaries’ invocation.

We have heard that the myriad spirits of Heaven and Earth, the manifold beings of yin and yang, rely upon the primordial harmony for nurturance and the Dao’s qi for generation and completion. The Three Destinies and Five Phases determine the reckoning of fortune and misfortune; the Southern Palace and Northern Bureau govern the records of transgression and blessing. No good or evil escapes their notice, nor the slightest measure goes unaccounted.

Moreover, as the Three Origins shift and the Nine Luminaries traverse their paths, omens of censure or favor manifest, their shadows answering as echoes. How could we fail to tremble with reverence and awe before the true numina?

This humble lady’s fate is governed by the earth and fire stars, moving through the position of *wu*. Not only does this mark her life’s station, but it also resides in her bodily palace. In the minor cycle of *chou*, it becomes one of the Six Harms; in the major cycle of *xu*, it falls upon the Tomb. In the major cycle, the *wu* fate weakens; in the minor, the kingly prosperity thins at its outset. Beset by such anxieties, we fear the onset of calamity.

Thus, with utmost sincerity, we turn in devotion to the celestial patterns. Following the rites of memorial presentation, we bow our heads to the Three Heavens; preparing the offerings for prayer and invocation, we direct our hearts toward the Nine Luminaries.

We implore the Most Perfect to show compassion, and the host of sages to bestow grace. Pardon the transgressions of past years, and dissolve the karmic debts of former lives. Pacify and dispel misfortune, rescue us from inauspicious decline. Prolong our years, augment our prosperity and blessings. May we ever receive your sheltering protection, and be granted enduring peace. We vow to serve the numinous spirits with unceasing devotion and reverence. In profound submission, we offer this prayer.

**Prayer for the Birthday Nanjou Offering of Lord Zongkui, Prefect of Yangzhou**

We have heard that the celestial bodies congeal their radiance, adorning the heavens with their signs. The Upper Palace of Southern Prosperity governs the Register of Life, bestowing blessings and flowing auspiciousness, subtly aiding state and realm. The *River Chart*’s secret admonitions elucidate the texts of reverent gaze; the *Zhengyi* sacred canons likewise preserve the principles of cultivation. Daring to unfold the mysterious teachings, we devoutly exhaust our sincerity.

Your servant has long received vast favor, personally encountering this glorious era. Abundant grace and honor have been bestowed, and I have trodden the path of imperial beneficence. Yet I possess no merit to aid the times or rectify the state, and presumptuously bear the weight of the ministerial seal and military insignia. Trembling with awe, I find it difficult to repay the bounty of creation; I vow to remain reverent and diligent, hoping to requite the virtue of sovereign and parents. Only through unceasing self-discipline do I dare not neglect my beginnings or endings.

Thus, on this birthday, I meticulously perform the offering rites. Bowing my head toward the cinnabar terrace, I fix my heart upon the mysterious pole. The sacred incense smoke ascends, seeking to reach the Nine Purities; in this propitious night, I offer earnest supplication, wishing to convey it before the Six Saints. Grant that your servant’s misfortunes and obstructions be dispelled, and enmities be harmoniously resolved. Augment my blessings and emoluments, prolong my years. Pardon past transgressions, and bestow future felicity. May the Primordial Mystery elevate and deliver me, and may my entire clan enjoy peace and well-being. I vow to uphold the utmost sincerity in reverence, forever aligning with the protection of the true numina. In profound submission, I offer this prayer.

---

**Prayer for the Completion of the Land Pacification Offering at the Hall of the Venerable One, Mount Qingcheng**

We have heard that when the Primordial Unity first divided, forms took shape through fusion. Among them, Mount Min, vast and encompassing the western frontiers, presses upon the two rivers as its guardian and crowns the Five Peaks in majesty. It is the dwelling of immortals, harboring grotto-heavens. Its layered peaks and towering ridges cradle the sun and moon amid the clouds; its piled verdure and stacked mists separate the dust of the mortal world from the celestial realm. Here, the heavenly realm gathers its true spirits, and the city of Chengdu flourishes with magic mushrooms and herbs. This is called the Court of Blessings, presiding over such sublime terrain.

The True Lord of Mystery and Tranquility, having attained the Dao in high antiquity, is renowned among the loftiest immortals. When the Xuanyuan Emperor made his southern progress, he honored the master-disciple rites; when the Brilliant Emperor journeyed west, he further adorned and embellished the site. The Han dynasty expanded the grand shrine, and on the *Zhonghe* day, a noble title was bestowed. Ever manifesting wondrous responses, it has greatly protected the realm.

Recently, I brushed aside the mist-laden vines to gaze upon the feathered banners, and the radiant countenance of the deity remained vivid in my mind, unforgotten in waking or dreaming. Of late, the gates and layered eaves have suffered from wind and rain, their decay and ruin a growing concern as the years silently pass. Thus, I commanded the Great Master Xingzhen to measure the timber, gather the craftsmen, and achieve this grand restoration. Gleaming eaves now catch the light, and jade-like waters cascade through the air. The murals on the four walls are renewed, and the steps and thresholds of the double railings remain unchanged. The main hall has been restored, forever broadcasting the mysterious favor.

May the deities of heaven, earth, mountains, and rivers, in their proper ranks and duties, continually bestow their blessings. Greatly shelter the multitudes, that violence and aggression may not intrude. Let no pestilence or plague arise, and may crops flourish abundantly. May wind and rain come in due season, the heavens be clear, and the land be adorned with jade and pearls. Let all within the four seas—Chinese and barbarian alike—witness civil refinement and martial repose. May border beacons fall silent, and malevolent forces be annihilated. May the scripts and chariots of all directions be united, and the calendars of the Nine Provinces be harmonized. May the people receive blessings, and the ancestral temples endure forever.

Thus, I diligently perform the rites of *pingzao*, ever offering fragrant sacrifices. I have dispatched Master Du Guangting of Broad Accomplishment to devoutly conduct the grand offering, luminously expressing gratitude to the true spirits. Gazing afar at the cloud-borne chariots, I reverently hope for the mysterious gaze. Respectfully, this prayer.

---

**Prayer for the Second Dispatch to Mount Qingcheng to Pacify and Restore the True Spirits**

We have heard that heaven establishes its sacred precincts, and earth opens its immortal courts. Here, the true spirits reside, revered in both the hidden and manifest realms. They grasp the guiding principles of the mountain ranges and govern the fortunes of all directions. Cloud-capped peaks and rosy-hued terraces have been venerated through the ages. Bestowing blessings upon the people, they have granted favors from antiquity to the present.

Recently, I ventured through distant vines and creepers to personally approach the august hall. Gazing upon the majestic bearing of the temple and the ceremonial guards of the four walls, the numinous presence seemed alive, and my reverence deepened. Thus, I commanded that the deities’ forms be painted and displayed within the inner hall. Morning saw the lighting of jade stalks, and evening the preparation of silver lamps. My prayers were earnest for the sake of the people, and my devotion was not confined to secret invocations. Trusting in the unfailing perception of the spirits, I am certain they have witnessed this sincerity.

Now, within the mountain temple, renovations have been completed. The halls have been renewed, and a separate offering has been commanded. Free from the taint of impure offerings, the rites possess an even greater purity and solemnity. Therefore, I specially perform this offering, meticulously preparing this declaration. I humbly invite the true spirits to return to their immortal abode. May their rainbow banners and crane-drawn chariots roam the pine and moonlight realms; may orchid fragrance and thoroughwort’s scent waft along the path of emptiness and non-being. May the true domain be eternally secure, and the state and realm receive great protection. From this time forth, may the people of the world forever await vast and boundless blessings. In utmost devotion, I offer this prayer. Respectfully, this prayer.

The seventeenth fascicle of the *Guangcheng Collection* is hereby concluded.
